Chapter 1275: Chapter 1274: Beyond the Boundary

From the cultivation of land with fire and homestead to the dynastic changes, inheritance has continued to the present day, and the Divine World has always hovered above, mysterious and unknown, the source of all legends.

Even the size of the Divine World remains unknown to the people, who cannot provide a precise answer.

When the Divine World unfolds, stars seem to come alive, breaking away from their orbits, becoming unpredictable, reverently welcoming the Divine World.

No legend, no theory, no experience can explain this phenomenon.

Facing the glimpse of sunlight revealed by the Divine World, there is a chorus of prayers throughout the White Horse Dynasty, seeking divine protection.

"Director, His Majesty has sent someone to inquire..." the Chief Clerk of the Imperial Astronomical Bureau reports.

The corner of the Director’s mouth twitches, his expression complex, unsure whether to cry or laugh: "What is he asking me? About the matters of the Divine World?"

Is this something I can explain?

Let alone me, even if all the past Directors were resurrected and gathered together, not one of them could explain it.

"Father, is that piece of the Divine World getting bigger?" his silent son suddenly speaks up.

The Director and the Chief Clerk both look up, with hearts already in turmoil now gripping their throats.

A fragment of the Divine World, occupying the entire view, is approaching them.

And when his son first noticed this fragment of the world, it was only the size of a sesame seed!

"The catastrophe of world destruction... is it."

The Director’s lips tremble, heart ashen, recognizing this as a natural calamity, insurmountable by anyone.

When this world fragment descends, it will mark the fall of the White Horse Dynasty; all dynastic transitions and political struggles become meaningless in this moment.

As they fall into despair, an indescribable giant hand appears, pinching the chunk of the world fragment as one would a pebble, halting its motion, suspended in place. frёeωebɳovel.com

The Director collapses on the ground, unable to exert the slightest bit of strength throughout his body.

The highs and lows he experienced in his life paled in comparison to tonight.

Before, he didn’t believe in the existence of immortals in this world, but now he feels it might be time to start believing.

...

"So this is what lies beyond the Box World," Lu Yang and others eagerly pass through the cracks from the Land of No Spirit, arriving at the universe.

In the vast cosmos, the Milky Way hangs inverted, stars glittering brilliantly, making life seem incredibly insignificant.

The stars are so close they seem within arm’s reach, as if a stretch of the hand could touch them.

Fragments of the Land of No Spirit explode beside them like fireworks.

At this moment, time stands still, and Lu Yang and his companions are intoxicated by the beautiful scene, unable to extricate themselves.

For Jiang Pingan and Meng Junzi, this is their first visit to the endless starry sky, and they feel their minds and hearts broaden.

The Immortal Fairy and other ancient cultivators are moved by the scene, reminiscing about the various aspects of ancient times.

Yun Zhi is no exception; as a child, her favorite thing to do was to lie down on the grass and watch the stars.

"Wait, why are there stars nearby?!" Lu Yang is the first to realize the problem. When the Four Ancient Immortals refined the stars into the continent, didn’t they refine all the stars within reach? Logically, there should be no stars near the Box World.

But reality clearly wasn’t so.

Now was not the time to admire the starry sky. The smallest fragments of the Land of No Spirit were made of hundreds of stars, and not a single star in the universe could withstand a collision with such a fragment.

It would be even worse if the fragment collided with a star that harbored life.

Lu Yang employed the Palm Buddha Country to catch the furthest flying fragment.

Seeing Lu Yang’s action, everyone else also realized that letting the Land of No Spirit fragments scatter was very dangerous and each began to use their Divine Abilities.

Law of Heaven and Earth, Demon Race true form, three heads and six arms, Rule Power... Everyone picked stars and grabbed moons, fixing all the fragments in place.

The Land of No Spirit fragments seemed about to crash into the stars at the last moment, but in reality, the two were far apart and posed no danger.

After the group recognized the potential risk, they easily eliminated it.

"I forgot that both the stars and the Box World are moving. The distribution of the stars from four hundred thousand years ago definitely differs from now." The Four Ancient Immortals arrived.

With the opening of the Box World, the dark clouds and thunder disappeared, and since people couldn’t see them anymore, there was no need for them to keep up appearances.

Qilin Immortal lay on a fragment of the continent, stretching like a cat: "The outside world is indeed more comfortable."

"Yes, in the outside world, whether it’s battling with spells or comprehending Divine Abilities, there’s no need to be concerned." Yingtian Immortal and others expressed.

The Box World was crowded with people, but once you reached the level of Immortals, any slight indiscretion could affect others nearby.

Out in the cosmos, it was different. You could just find any desolate star and do whatever you wanted without much concern.

In the various continents of the Cultivation World, whether Human race or Demon Race, everyone was talking excitedly about the cosmos that had been revealed just before the clouds disappeared.

"Is that what lies beyond our world? It feels similar to the starry sky we usually see," a Junior Cultivator scoffed, feeling disappointed after his unnecessary excitement.

His elder was a Divinity Transformation Cultivator, who knew much more: "That’s because your Cultivation Level is too low. The outside world is far larger than our Box World, a fact that is more obvious the higher one’s cultivation is. Besides, the outside world contains real stars."

Integration Period Cultivators grouped together, rubbing their hands in eagerness, ready for a big undertaking: "The seal has finally been lifted, now let’s proceed with the plan we agreed upon before!"

Three Integration Period Cultivators went to the Imperial City, located the Outer Realm Investigation Department established by Great Xia, queued up, collected application forms, filled out personal information, team intentions, guarantees, then submitted their forms, and waited for the review.

Most staffing the Outer Realm Investigation Department were Luoshui Guards. Since the issues with the demonic sect and Ancient Cultivators had been resolved, their workload had significantly decreased. As the department mainly dealt with High Level Cultivators and was short-staffed, the Dynasty transferred them here.

Similar organizations existed in Buddha Country, East Sea, and Demon Territory, decided upon by Emperor Xia, Demon Emperor, and others in a meeting. The objective was for cultivators to orderly venture into the outside world.

Yu Qian, one of the Nine Palaces of the Luoshui Guards, reminded these Integration Period Cultivators before they left: "Congratulations, your application to travel outside has been approved. Don’t forget the newly enacted inter-realm laws, as well as the guarantee you signed."

"If you violate the regulations outside, we will bring you to justice no matter where you flee, even to the ends of the earth."

"Of course, of course, Daoist Yu is aware of our character. We guarantee not to cause any troubles," the three Integration Period Cultivators said, their faces brimming with a smile so wide they couldn’t hide it, not expecting their application to pass so quickly.

The three brothers by oath, close as anything, teamed up and flew up from Great Xia, passing through an Array Method, and smoothly entered the outside world.

This Array Method would automatically identify the objects they brought with them upon leaving and those they returned with. It also served to prevent the dissipation of Spiritual Energy from the Box World into the external world.

"So this is the outside world, it’s so vast," remarked the leader, casually brushing aside a star obstructing his view.

"But the lack of Spiritual Energy in the outside world is a significant problem."

"We’ll just have to conserve Spiritual Energy then. We can rely on our physical bodies to travel and leap between stars."

"That’s true. Let’s first check out the nearby stars and see if there are any living creatures on them."

"Caution is key; life forms from the outside might be stronger than all three of us combined."

Chapter 1276: Chapter 1275: White Horse Dynasty

"I didn’t expect that there were living creatures so close to our world." Lu Yang changed into the clothes of the White Horse Dynasty and strolled in the street with his hands in his pockets.

Lu Yang was among the first batch of cultivators to leave the outer world, and didn’t require any approval process.

Upon arriving in the outer world, everyone was very excited, flying in different directions to see what the outer world was really like.

By chance, Lu Yang found a star nearby.

"Is that the White Horse Dynasty with a thousand years of history? Interesting."

Lu Yang temporarily named this star the White Horse Star.

After a brief investigation, he roughly figured out the situation of the White Horse Star.

The White Horse Dynasty is the largest kingdom on this star, with the surrounding minor kingdoms either being vassals of the White Horse Dynasty or too far away, just beginning to form their own concept of a nation.

Here, the spiritual energy is extremely thin, making it difficult even for Energy Introduction into the body, so the people have taken a different approach, walking a path similar to body refinement, the path of martial masters.

The three most powerful martial masters include the Martial Arts Alliance Hierarch, the Dynasty General, and the Inner Leader, who can lift massive stones weighing hundreds of pounds, and are regarded as divine beings by the people!

"The Divine World they talk about in their legends is probably our world."

"They must have seen the breaking of the Land of No Spirit, frightened by it. We should also meet the Emperor and explain things clearly to avoid any unnecessary panic."

"Why not just explain directly to them? Why do an investigation?" Fairy Eternity didn’t understand.

Lu Yang shook his head: "Since we’ve come with the intention of cultural exchange, we should respect their customs and understand their history and culture. This way, the chance of misunderstanding is reduced when we communicate with them."

"After all, we are now representing the Cultivation World, and first impressions are important. We can’t be arrogant or condescending."

Fairy Eternity sounded an ’oh’ but didn’t really understand what Little Yang was talking about.

She pointed in the direction of the Imperial Palace: "I think their communication is quite efficient. I was wondering if you could learn something from them."

At that moment, a terrifying aura erupted from the White Horse Dynasty Imperial Palace.

...

The White Horse Dynasty court meeting.

After last night’s terrifying events, from the Emperor to the ministers, everyone was in a state of panic.

They all wanted to know what exactly happened last night. Did a divine being manifest?

They used their connections to ask the astrologers but still couldn’t get an answer.

"Minister Wang, about last night’s anomaly in the Divine World, what was the cause? Is it a blessing or a curse?" The Emperor had asked Director Wang several times last night, and Director Wang could only appease him by saying it was a sign of good fortune.

So, at the morning court, the Emperor asked him to repeat it in front of all the civil and military officials.

Director Wang smiled bitterly in his heart, praying it was truly a good omen. If any disaster happened soon, his career as Director was over.

The ministers were eager to hear Director Wang’s answer.

"Your Majesty..." Just as Director Wang was about to repeat last night’s lines, a hearty laugh interrupted.

"That must be something good!" Three figures suddenly appeared, hovering above the palace, radiating strange brilliance, incredibly divine, like the deities of legend.

"Protect His Majesty!"

The Inner Leader quickly surrounded the Emperor with his men, watching the three figures warily.

Seeing the Inner Leader, the three figures smiled: "Looks like you are Zhang Longhan, one of the three great masters of the White Horse Dynasty, who can lift hundreds of pounds of stone, eh?"

"Don’t be nervous, we have no ill intent."

Seeing that everyone was still tense and did not believe their words.

One of them snapped his fingers, and everyone unexpectedly began to float uncontrollably, even Zhang Longhan was powerless to resist.

The strength he took pride in was nothing compared to these three, who rendered him merely a commoner!

The man snapped his fingers again, and everyone landed safely.

Flying, this what Immortals can do, no matter how strong a martial master is, they can’t fly!

"Let me introduce ourselves. We three are Integration Period Cultivators from Great Xia. My name is Sui Han, founder of the First Class Sect Sui Han Sect, and these two are Daoist Xuan Yi and Daoist Wen."

Initially, the three of them planned to proceed cautiously, but after discovering the existence of the White Horse Dynasty, they realized they were worried for nothing as nothing here posed a threat to them.

"The incident last night was also unexpected for us. To put it simply, four great figures unraveled the world’s seal, allowing us to leave our world."

The officials and the Emperor couldn’t imagine who could be referred to as "great figures" by these three.

"So it was like that," the Emperor stuttered in response.

Sui Han looked at the Emperor enthusiastically: "Actually, we have a small proposal. We see that there are many people in your White Horse Dynasty, and surely there are many with the aptitude for cultivation but lacking Spiritual Energy."

"Would you be able to gather all the children of the dynasty, so we can test for Spirit Roots? If they wish to cultivate, they could come to our sect in the White Horse Dynasty to cultivate!"

Although Sui Han Sect is a First Class Sect, it is very ordinary amongst such sects, and located near Immortal Gate Prison Sect and the Super-grade Control Qi Sect, they have no competitive edge in recruitment.

If they could lure some promising disciples to their Sect before other powers discovered this place, it would be the greatest achievement of their journey.

Seeing that the Emperor and ministers were all in a daze, Daoist Xuan Yi sent a telepathic message to Sui Han: "Older brother, you forgot to mention the benefits."

"Oh right, I was so excited I forgot about that."

Sui Han cleared his throat: "After all, gathering the children is not easy for you, so how about this, whatever demands you have, we can fulfill."

"Any demand?" the Emperor asked cautiously, afraid to offend the immortals.

"Could you help us solve the problem of rising sea levels?"

"That’s no issue, I’ll just cast a spell to freeze part of the sea, build an ice continent, and the water will naturally recede."

Freezing a part of the sea was an easy task for Sui Han, hardly a demand: "Any other demands?"

"Can you help us deal with the Calamity Star? Director said it is because of the existence of the Calamity Star that our dynasty suffers constant natural disasters."

"Is the Calamity Star an actual star? Where is it?" Daoist Sui Han stroked his chin, finding the issue quite challenging.

The Director hurriedly took out the Stargazing Map and pointed out the direction to Daoist Sui Han.

It was the first time Daoist Sui Han had seen the Stargazing Map, and he was very intrigued: "This map is quite good; can I buy a copy from you?"

They were just worrying about not knowing the way outside, and here a map was delivered right to their doorstep; indeed, doing good deeds has its rewards.

"Give it to you, give it to you," the Emperor repeatedly said.

Daoist Sui Han and his two companions studied for a long time before they understood the Stargazing Map and the location of the Calamity Star.

He performed the Big and Small Ruyi, opened his large hand, and lifted the roof of the Imperial Palace: "The Calamity Star is in that direction, right?"

It was dawn at the moment, with a dim light in the sky, and the starry sky could still be seen clearly, with the Calamity Star twinkling.

In fact, this was a normal astronomical phenomenon, but none of the people present understood that.

Daoist Sui Han’s Life-bound Magical Treasure was the Ice Bow. He drew the Ice Bow, condensed Ice Arrows, and fired one straight at the Calamity Star.

Before long, under the watchful eyes of the crowd, the Calamity Star exploded and disappeared from sight.

"Not bad, not too difficult, all done," Daoist Sui Han said with a smile.

Everyone was so scared that they sat down on the ground. What kind of divine powers were these? Drawing a bow to shoot a star was completely beyond their comprehension, it was like witnessing a myth come to life.

Suddenly, three Flood Dragons appeared above the Imperial Palace.

"Dragons! They’re dragons!" cried a minister. In their legends, dragons were auspicious.

Daoist Sui Han and his two friends frowned; they recognized these three dragons as members of the East Sea Flood Dragon Clan. Had they also found this place?

"To think that there are so many mortals here." The leading Flood Dragon, as if he did not see Daoist Sui Han, transformed into human form and helped the Emperor up.

"I did not mean to scare you, my apologies."

"No, no problem."

"I presume Daoist Sui Han has already discussed our situation with you. I wonder if your territory would be willing to accept the protection of our Flood Dragon Clan?"

"With our protection, we could teach you the methods for longevity and cultivation, among many other benefits."

Daoist Sui Han and his two friends frowned: "Accepting protection is another form of territorial expansion. Do you want to make the White Horse Dynasty your territory? That is not permissible!"

The Flood Dragon smiled and said: "If it’s mutually agreeable, why can’t it be done?"

"This White Horse Dynasty is suitable, just right for relocating our people here."

Then three Integration Period Cultivators appeared, emitting an almost imperceptible chill.

Flood Dragons frowned: "Cultivators from the Extreme Northern Lands?"

They rarely dealt with people from the Extreme Northern Lands.

The three Integration Period Cultivators from the Extreme Northern Lands approached the Emperor: "Are you the Emperor here? We intend to relocate some of our people to your territory."

"Daoist, you’re overstepping your bounds," the Flood Dragon warned. The White Horse Dynasty was their territory; how could they accept people from the Extreme Northern Lands?

The cultivators from the Extreme Northern Lands sneered: "Overstepping? You just said it yourself, if it’s mutual, what’s the problem?"

The atmosphere in the Imperial Palace suddenly turned icy cold, with three parties’ forces, nine Body Integration Realm Cultivators, all eyeing the White Horse Dynasty.

"Do we fight?" ƒreewebnσvel.com

"Who’s afraid?"

"Then bring it on!"

None of the three parties’ forces was willing to back down; their gazes were cold as they started manipulating their Profound Skills.

The Emperor and his ministers, terrified by this scene, scrambled frantically to flee.

"Oh, let’s see who wants to fight?"

The youth leaned against the door frame, smiling but not laughing, his gaze fixed on the nine Integration Period Cultivators.

"Who!"

Upon clearly seeing the youth’s appearance, the nine Integration Period Cultivators felt as if they had been doused with cold water, instantly simmering down.

Lu Yang!

Lu Yang helped the fallen Director to his feet and walked toward the three parties’ forces with a smile.

"Quite imposing, aren’t we? Forgot the rules, did we?"

"Exploring outside, try not to disturb the creatures on the stars, remember?"

"One came to pick Spirit Roots, one to encircle land, and one to colonize; all very capable, indeed!"

Faced with Lu Yang’s admonishment, the nine Integration Period Cultivators hung their heads, not daring to reply.

In their eyes, the Lu Yang of today was not just among the first Geniuses, but a genuine Transcendence Tribulation Stage Cultivator, an existence they dared not provoke.

In the eyes of the Emperor and his ministers, Lu Yang was shrouded in a mysterious veil.

These nine divine beings had the power to reach the heavens, yet in the presence of this youth, they were so frightened they couldn’t even speak.

Who exactly was he?!

"Sending you out was to let you see what the outside world is like, not to give you a chance to flex your power!"

Lu Yang turned around, just about to reassure the Emperor, saying that we pursue peace, and with me here, nothing will happen.

Then he saw the Emperor respectfully lifting the Imperial Jade Seal above his head: "My lord, our White Horse Dynasty is willing to submit to you."

Lu Yang: "..."

No, I’m not here for that.

Chapter 1277: Chapter 1276: The Great Bean Dynasty Expands Its Territory Today

"Little Yang, keep it, keep it, it’s just right for them to join our Great Bean Dynasty." Fairy Eternity in the Spiritual Space was egging Lu Yang on, relentlessly whispering in his ear.

"You can consider this expanding the territory; I’ll credit you with a great merit."

Although Lu Yang was a Pillar Minister of the Great Bean Dynasty, he had his own thoughts and couldn’t just listen to whatever Fairy Eternity said.

He appeared in the Imperial Palace to stop the fight in the name of justice, not to mark territory or claim land. What kind of talk would that be if word got out? It would contradict his upright and dignified image.

Lu Yang put the Imperial Jade Seal back into the Emperor’s hand and explained calmly: "Our Great Bean Dynasty is not recruiting anyone."

"The Great Bean Dynasty?" The Emperor was taken aback, finding the name odd.

Lu Yang inwardly cursed, realizing his slip-up was due to Fairy Eternity’s constant murmuring about the Great Bean Dynasty in the Spiritual Space, now occupying his thoughts.

"I mean, we come for peace, respecting your wishes absolutely, guaranteeing your independence, and you won’t become a vassal to anybody."

The Emperor sincerely wished to submit to Lu Yang—that simply had to be done. Although he didn’t understand what was so good about their White Horse Dynasty for it to attract nine Divine beings in such a short time, if it weren’t for this Immortal’s arrival, he couldn’t begin to imagine the consequences.

Just as Lu Yang was about to explain further to reassure the Emperor, the sky resounded with the sonorous chanting of Buddhist scriptures.

"Well said, it’s unexpected to encounter a star with living beings, all mere mortals, upon my arrival. It’s truly a godsend and perfect for my Dharma assembly..."

The monk from Buddha Country saw the nine at the Body Integration Realm in the Imperial Palace and Lu Yang who was supporting the Emperor, and his voice abruptly stopped, sweating profusely.

The Emperor quietly watched Lu Yang, while Lu Yang silently looked up at the monk from Buddha Country in the sky.

Trying to cause trouble, huh? I just finished stating our peaceful intentions, and on the heels of that, you come and treat this place as your Dharma assembly?

"Amitabha, this poor monk will take his leave now."

"Come back." Lu Yang said just two words, scaring the high monk from Buddha Country into retreating back in the air.

"Benefactor Lu, ah no, Senior Lu, perhaps there’s some misunderstanding here."

Lu Yang ignored the monk, making him stand with the nine at the Body Integration Realm as punishment, while he continued to soothe the Emperor.

"They are just new to the outer world, emotionally unsettled, and inevitably made some inappropriate actions. Rest assured, I’ll report back on your kingdom’s situation soon, and they will send people over to ensure everything is taken care of."

Lu Yang was quite confident in the work ethics of Great Xia.

"As for the seniors, please cease your exploration and come back with me."

Lu Yang’s eyes narrowed slightly, exuding a strand of imposing pressure, staring at the ten at the Body Integration Realm with a displeased look. They had just left and already caused such a mess, tarnishing the outer world’s impression of them. Those unaware might even think they were bandits.

Sui Han Daoist and the other two had a relatively minor issue and just needed to copy the laws a few times as punishment. As for the others, certainly, they would not be allowed to go out anymore.

The ten at the Body Integration Realm felt the imposing pressure released by Lu Yang, their expressions changing dramatically.

This kind of pressure was definitely not what one at the Early Tribulation Stage should possess!

Could it be that he has already cultivated to the Middle Tribulation Stage?!

It hadn’t been long, the speed of his cultivation was frighteningly swift.

Naturally, they were reluctant to return, but no one dared to flee.

After bidding farewell to the Emperor, Lu Yang led the ten at the Body Integration Realm back to Great Xia, first sending Sui Han and his companions back, then informing the Outer Realm Investigation Department about the White Horse Dynasty, instructing them to send help immediately.

After that, Lu Yang visited the Western Paradise Temple of Buddha Country, the Dragon Palace of the East Sea, and the Snow Emperor at the Extreme Northern Lands, one after another.

"Good for nothing, daring to ignore my words!" The Snow Emperor roared in anger, frightening the three at the Body Integration Realm from the Extreme Northern Lands into trembling.

"Fellow Daoist Lu Yang, I didn’t expect you to be at the Transcendance Tribulation Stage already," Xue Shilou smiled and said. He was currently following the Snow Emperor in cultivation, and seeing the rapid pace of Lu Yang’s cultivation, he couldn’t help feeling envious.

But he also knew that all he could do was envy Lu Yang; comparing their cultivation was simply humiliating himself.

"Snow Daoist, do cultivate diligently, but don’t be overly hasty," Lu Yang kindly advised.

...

After Lu Yang left, the Emperor and his ministers were extremely anxious, fearing the appearance of more divine beings.

And as if their fears summoned the very occurrence, soon new deities arrived, leaving the ministers almost numb.

"There indeed is a dynasty close by."

The newcomers were three people, with the leader noticing the expressions of the Emperor and his ministers, he said: "Don’t be nervous. I am Yu Qian from the Great Xia Outer Realm Investigation Department. My colleagues here are with me, sent by Lu Yang."

The group, originally tense, felt somewhat relieved to hear that the visitors were introduced by Lu Yang.

"Immortal, please take a seat," the Emperor instructed the eunuchs to bring seats and ordered the Imperial Kitchen to quickly prepare a feast to entertain the Immortal.

"There is no need for such trouble; we are here to understand some matters."

Lu Yang had only provided an introduction to the situation of the White Horse Dynasty to the Outer Realm Investigation Department, and Yu Qian and his colleagues were here for a more thorough investigation.

After all, the White Horse Dynasty is the first power encountered since breaking the seal; one cannot be too cautious.

The problems encountered during interaction with the White Horse Dynasty are very helpful in establishing new exploration principles subsequently.

"Immortal, please ask away, I will withhold nothing."

One of Yu Qian’s colleagues took out paper and pen to record, while another produced a Recording Orb to capture this historic moment.

"Is your power called the White Horse Dynasty?"

"Yes."

"How long is its history?"

"One thousand two hundred years exactly." The Emperor was very proud when talking about the history of the White Horse Dynasty, for it had been the longest ruling dynasty through ancient and modern times.

Yu Qian had never seen a dynasty ruling for such a short period, almost like it had just been established, but judging from the other party’s expression, they seemed very proud of one thousand two hundred years.

It seemed that the concept of time regarding the founding of a mortal nation was different from theirs; perhaps this was a very worthy question for research, so he temporarily noted this point down.

"Have you then ever made contact with beings from beyond this star?"

"Star? You mean the place we’re in is a star?" The Emperor was shocked, and the previously quiet ministers also became restless.

They had always believed that their world was a flat continent, after all, the Divine World above was the best example of that.

Yu Qian thought to himself, it seems they have not made contact with beings from other stars.

"How many inhabitants does your dynasty have?"

The Life Star seemed to exhibit extreme polarization; one side was lush and vibrant with life, while the other was bare and devoid of greenery.

Steering the Black Canopy Boat to the lively side, Lu Yang arbitrarily chose a spot to dock.

After disembarking, Lu Yang discovered the environment was somewhat similar to the Demon Territory, with towering trees reaching the clouds, densely covering the sky, and the air was humid and sweltering.

It was almost like a tropical rainforest.

"It seems there are signs of the Human race’s activities here?"

Lu Yang had not walked far when he found human-built structures, long abandoned and overgrown with vines.

"Such exquisite architecture," commented Fairy Eternity. The structure was neither wooden nor stone; it was complex, unlike anything she had seen before.

"It is indeed exquisite, like the architecture from before I crossed over," Lu Yang said, touching the abandoned building with a hint of emotion. The architectural style resembled that of Blue Star, distinctly "modern."

"Ah? Could this be the star you originally came from?"

"That’s impossible."

"Why?"

Lu Yang pointed at the sign posted at the entrance of the building: "Because the text on it is unfamiliar to me."

"It looks like the technology of this star is quite advanced, but it’s unknown why it has been abandoned."

Just as Lu Yang was about to use his Spiritual Sense to inspect the star, he suddenly heard a roaring noise.

Roar—

A several zhang tall, vibrant tiger strode forward, its tail like a long whip, lightly sweeping, and towering trees were snapped in half by its tremendous force.

Lu Yang was stunned: "Are the tigers here this big?"

Lu Yang attempted to communicate with the tiger, but although it was massive, it was not yet at the stage of developing Spiritual Wisdom—just a fierce wild beast.

The tiger roared again, pouncing towards Lu Yang.

Lu Yang let out a slight sigh, wondering why he was being attacked just upon arriving at this star, feeling it to be quite unfriendly towards him.

He flicked his fingers casually, and Sword Qi pierced through the tiger’s skull, snuffing out its life.

"Speaking of which, there are quite a lot of wild beasts on this star, encountering such a large tiger so casually."

...

The fully armed Salvation Team moved quietly through the jungle.

"How far away are we from the Beast King?" they whispered to each other, afraid of alerting their target.

"According to the intelligence we gathered, the King of Mutant Beasts is still five hundred meters away."

The captain nodded silently, saying nothing more.

Each of them had a determined look, ready to face death.

Thirty years have passed since the great disaster, and in the last three decades, the Mutant Beasts have occupied half of the land on this star, with human territory dwindling daily.

At this rate, humanity will surely be extinct!

To counter this, the human elites gathered seven out of the top ten experts to form the Salvation Team to deal with the troublesome King of Mutant Beasts.

The team leader, named Zhan Po, was ranked first among the top ten experts in chaotic times. He seldom spoke, but his every word and deed influenced the team, truly deserving the title of boss.

Zhan Po’s child perished at the hands of the Mutant Beasts, prompting him to vow to annihilate all Mutant Beasts!

The deputy leader, named Shi Lingyun, was the youngest of the top ten experts with the highest talent. Although his appointment as deputy leader was controversial, since he defeated another one of the top ten experts, no one questioned his role.

Shi Lingyun was at the bottom of his class at school, but by chance, he came into contact with an Enhancer. Normally, Enhancers had side effects, but Shi Lingyun was naturally immune, attracting significant attention from human leadership.

However, his fiancée was the daughter of a high-ranking human authority and was very beautiful. Before Shi Lingyun became one of the top ten experts, many sought trouble with him over this.

One of the team members, named Yuan Xing, frequently joked and livened up the team’s mood, but Shi Lingyun saw him gazing at a photo toward the sky with an expression of Sadness on a quiet night, obviously harboring an untold past.

Another member, named Su Tianxing, whose father was one of the former top ten experts, worked tirelessly to prove himself and eventually became one of the new top ten experts. He often clashed with Shi Lingyun, but after jointly defending against a swarm of beasts, they became confidants.

The King of Mutant Beasts was shrouded in mystery, with its race unknown—only that it was extremely powerful, commanding all Mutant Beasts.

After sacrificing countless lives, humans barely managed to determine the location of the King of Mutant Beasts.

"Lingyun, if we fail this battle, we will cover your escape," said team leader Zhan Po.

"Captain!" Shi Lingyun was somewhat agitated.

Zhan Po pressed down on Shi Lingyun’s shoulder, his tone resolute: "Listen to me, I know you’re not afraid to die, but no one knows how strong the King of Mutant Beasts really is. Should we fail, you are our last hope for humanity, you cannot fall no matter what!"

"Enough, let’s stop talking, we have arrived."

Their life detectors indicated the presence of life ahead.

They exchanged glances and continued forward—the King of Mutant Beasts was right in front of them!

They parted some leaves and saw the corpse of a vibrant tiger as large as a small hill.

And atop that hill, sat a young man in strange attire.

Their expressions grew solemn, never before feeling such pressure, an indescribable fear spreading among them.

The King of Mutant Beasts... was actually humanoid!

Chapter 1282: Chapter 1281: Lu Yang felt they were so noisy

Before this, the Salvation Team made many assumptions, guessing the King of Mutant Beasts could be a tiger, lion, elephant, or a combination of various animals.

They devised combat plans for various scenarios.

But they never anticipated that the King of Mutant Beasts would be humanoid!

How was this achieved? Is it mimicry, or some other yet undiscovered ability?

A chill ran up from the soles of their feet to their skulls, stemming from the fear of the unknown.

Would their guns and swords still be effective?

The captain signaled with a gesture, meaning to prepare for a surprise attack based on the original plan!

At this point, panicking is useless; they can only fight for their lives to secure a bright future for humanity!

At the very least, they must severely injure the King of Mutant Beasts to buy some breathing time for mankind!

"Oh, what a coincidence to find someone in this place."

The King of Mutant Beasts, sitting atop a fierce tiger, waved and smiled over here. Lu Yang was somewhat surprised; it was not strange to find tigers in this desolate place, but humans too?

This is Spiritual Sense transmission, communicating through thoughts, allowing one’s words to automatically convert into a language the other party can understand.

Not only is it humanoid, it can also speak!

"It has spotted us, attack now!"

The captain temporarily changed the combat plan to an aggressive assault.

He took the lead, pulling out a high-power Laser Sword, a pinnacle of human technological achievement that cost a fortune to create for him; this Laser Sword could slice through steel and concrete as easily as tofu!

No wonder he’s the top among the ten masters; his movements were as fast as thunder, reaching the King of Mutant Beasts in the blink of an eye!

"I’ll cover you!"

A burly man said in a rough voice; he was known as the "Weapon Expert" among the top ten masters, carrying various highly lethal weapons, even the captain Zhan Po didn’t dare to confront him head-on.

Countless shells were fired, striking the King of Mutant Beasts with earth-shattering force!

Shi Lingyun, nicknamed "Will of Lingyun," was a master of Ancient Martial Arts. He charged second, not using weapons, for his fists and feet were his weapons!

"Monkey King" Yuan Xing, "Second Under Heaven" Su Tianxing, "Hundred Battles" Gai Xiao...

Seven of the top ten masters acted simultaneously, creating an extremely shocking scene; each one was a mighty warrior capable of holding a city alone, with the combined power of the seven, being an event unparalleled in human history!

"Why do you attack everyone you see?" Lu Yang frowned, grabbing the Laser Sword with his bare hands.

"What?!"

Captain Zhan Po’s pupils dilated; for the first time, his Laser Sword was blocked, and it was even being gripped!

Moreover, after a round of shelling from the Weapon Expert, not a single scratch appeared on the King of Mutant Beasts?!

"Mountain Shifting Fist!"

Shi Lingyun attacked from the side, fully unleashing his Ancient Martial Arts; his fist could shake mountains, yet it made Lu Yang stand unwavering!

"Could you be mistaking me for someone else? Also, don’t hit people randomly."

Lu Yang flicked his fingers, sending Shi Lingyun flying.

Shi Lingyun rocketed backwards, his pupils filled with astonishment.

"Lingyun, get out of here!" Captain Zhan Po decisively shouted; they had used their most powerful techniques in the shortest time, yet they barely scratched the King of Mutant Beasts.

The King of Mutant Beasts was far stronger than anyone anticipated, and they definitely weren’t able to defeat him!

"I won’t!" Shi Lingyun’s eyes reddened, "Leaving me alone to survive, I can’t do that!"

"Not telling you to just survive, you are the hope of the human race, if you don’t leave everyone will die here!" Zhan Po said angrily.

"It’s not like you guys are making me look like the bad guy." Lu Yang helplessly complained, what kind of people are these, attacking as soon as they meet, even the Demon Territory is not this chaotic.

But then again, just a random exploration team is so strong, the human race of this star is quite impressive.

Seeing Lu Yang stand up, team members all tried to stop him.

Seeing one teammate after another being sent flying, Shi Lingyun was tearful, remembering all the past moments, there were arguments and disagreements, but also laughter and joy, he had to protect everything!

He screamed until his voice cracked, stomping the ground: "No—"

Zhan Po revealed an incredulous scene, then burst into joy.

This is the state of fully absorbing the Enhancer, and also theoretically the strongest state, even he is a Half Step behind!

He had originally wanted Shi Lingyun to go back and regroup, fully absorb the Enhancer, and then fight again, but now he had fully absorbed it!

Shi Lingyun’s aura was imposing, his body stronger than ever, staring at Lu Yang with bloodshot eyes, he said emphatically:

"I, will, defeat, you!"

At this moment, Shi Lingyun is the strongest of the human race, the victory in battle, the hope of his teammates, the future of humanity, he carried too much, these were both his pressure and his motivation!

"Lingyun!"

Teammates shouted excitedly, finally seeing a hope for victory.

Everyone present was extremely excited, tears streaming, except Lu Yang who found them very noisy.

Lu Yang: "..."

Tried to fight upon meeting, thinking of running when unable to fight, halfway through running thinking they could fight and turned back to continue hitting me, and each one of them so excited, are you guys sick?

"Quiet."

Lu Yang snapped his fingers in the air, and sent Shi Lingyun flying again, everyone fell into despair.

Even Shi Lingyun, evolved to the strongest state, is not able to match the King of Mutant Beasts?

He walked leisurely to the front of the crowd, showing a smile he thought was kind: "Can we sit down and talk nicely now?"

...

Soon, the Salvation Team was sitting neatly in front of Lu Yang.

"Are you saying, thirty years ago a mad scientist conducted illegal experiments and developed an Evolution Potion, causing animals to evolve collectively, taking over your planet?"

"You refer to these evolved animals as Mutant Beasts, the King of Mutant Beasts can control all the Mutant Beasts, things like your nuclear bombs were intercepted by the birds among the Mutant Beasts, so they couldn’t be launched."

"After paying a heavy price, humans held onto half of the territory."

"You are the top ten masters of humans, specifically here to deal with the King of Mutant Beasts, and then you mistook me for the King of Mutant Beasts?"

The Salvation Team nodded in unison.

Lu Yang patted the big tiger beneath him: "So this is the King of Mutant Beasts?"

"Uh, it should be, after all, we don’t know what the King of Mutant Beasts looks like."

Lu Yang suddenly realized, wondering why the tiger he encountered casually was so powerful, it turns out it’s the King of Mutant Beasts, this team is not just any exploration team, but the top ten masters of humans.

"Lucky for me, if you had encountered this tiger, at least half of you would have died, provided this guy called Shi Lingyun had breakthrough."

Captain Zhan Po noticed the hole in the tiger’s forehead, breaking into a cold sweat, the human race’s helpless King of Mutant Beasts couldn’t even withstand a single move from him, who exactly is this person!

"This Mr. Lu... who exactly are you?"

The terrifying parts of Lu Yang had completely surpassed his imagination, who is this person, a legendary immortal, or a hermit expert?

"Me? I’m just out travelling."

Chapter 1283: Chapter 1282: One Sword Annihilates the Mutant Beasts

"Travel, travel?!" Captain Zhan Po thought he had heard wrong and couldn’t keep up with the conversation.

Lu Yang pointed backwards at the Black Canopy Boat: "Look, that’s my boat."

The members of the Salvation Team nearly popped their eyeballs out when they saw the Black Canopy Boat.

When Lu Yang mentioned he had a boat, they imagined a spacecraft with a metallic sheen, full of a futuristic and technological vibe.

But they never expected it to be just an ordinary boat.

This kind of boat would be featured at the beginning of history books!

"Right, you said this big tiger is the King of Mutant Beasts, able to control all Mutant Beasts. Now that it’s dead, what will happen to the Mutant Beasts, will they just die off?"

Zhan Po shook his head: "The most challenging aspect of dealing with Mutant Beasts is their organized actions. With the King of Mutant Beasts dead, we humans have the chance to break them one by one."

Zhan Po’s tone was decisive, his expression full of longing and expectation: "Ten years, at most ten years, and we humans will be able to reclaim Sky Sea Star, which rightfully belongs to us!"

The Salvation Team imagined the future and couldn’t help but smile.

Lu Yang also smiled and said, "Ten years is too long. Let me give you a hand."

Before the Salvation Team could react, Lu Yang stood up, drew out his Green Peak Sword, and with their jaws dropped in astonishment, he lifted off the ground and took flight.

Even the ever-talkative Yuan Xing was rendered speechless at the moment.

"Captain, can people actually fly?" Shi Lingyun nudged the captain. He had evolved to the utmost, so why couldn’t he fly?

And he didn’t have any wings, so how could he fly?

"Don’t ask me, I don’t know either."

Lu Yang soared through the clouds, arriving above Sky Sea Star, his Spiritual Sense spread out, covering the entire star, locking onto all Mutant Beasts.

Every Mutant Beast on this star was under Lu Yang’s full surveillance—the Beast Tide attacking cities, soldiers fighting to the death, and generals sharing their fate with their city.

Three of the top ten masters among the humans were among them, resisting the Beast Tide.

Even though the big tiger was dead and the Mutant Beasts had lost control, their bloodlust had been ignited in battle, and even without someone to control them, they would still attack the cities.

Mutant Beasts weren’t only on land but also in the sea, and there were several in the ocean on par with the big tiger, as well as one more powerful than the big tiger.

Perhaps that one in the ocean was the real King of Mutant Beasts; only the human elites and the Salvation Team were unaware of its existence.

"One Sword Becomes Ten Thousand."

The Green Peak Sword traced an arc in the sky, leaving behind an indelible sword image that spread like wildfire at an incredible speed.

If someone were in outer space, they would see Sky Sea Star coated in a golden sheen—that was the gleaming light of countless Green Peak Swords.

Using his index and middle fingers together, the immense Spiritual Sense locked onto every Mutant Beast, a sword image hovering above each of their heads.

He simply exhaled one word.

"Fall."

Sword images like scattered light, raining down like swords, the sword shadows acting like divine punishment, indiscriminately piercing through every bloodthirsty Mutant Beast.

No matter if it was the ordinary Mutant Beasts on land or the true King of Mutant Beasts hidden in the deep sea, each required only one sword image.

Feeling the threat to its life, the King of Mutant Beasts in the ocean tried desperately to escape. However, golden sword shadows descended from the heavens, plunging into the sea, and instead of slowing down, their speed increased even more.

The King of Mutant Beasts twisted its tentacles to fend off the attack.

Boom—

A mist of blood spread, and this King of Mutant Beasts, having not yet wreaked havoc in the human world, died at the bottom of the sea never reached by humans.

The Salvation Team did not know what Lu Yang, soaring through the sky, was planning to do. They were in the territory of the great tiger, with no mutant beasts nearby. All they could see was a distant descent of golden light.

Then, a hissing noise came through their communication channel, from the three Masters tasked with defending the city.

"Zhan Po, have you succeeded!?"

"The King of Mutant Beasts has been killed by you!"

"How did you do it? Swords, so many golden swords descended from the sky, killing all the mutant beasts!"

The city-defending human Masters spoke with an excited and incoherent tone. Knowing that the Salvation Team had gone to kill the King of Mutant Beasts, they naturally connected this event with the Salvation Team.

The Salvation Team looked at each other, shock and fear in their eyes.

What kind of method was this?!

Lu Yang landed with a smile, sheathing his Green Peak Sword: "Done."

"Mr. Lu..."

Lu Yang raised his hand to interrupt Shi Lingyun: "Let’s talk while we walk. Along the way, tell me your stories and show me around your city. If I could meet your President, that would be even better."

"That’s a given, that’s a given," Shi Lingyun hurriedly said. Even if Mr. Lu didn’t mention it, the President would take the initiative to meet him.

Seeing that Zhan Po was about to speak but hesitated, glancing at the great tiger’s corpse, Lu Yang understood what he meant.

He used the Identity Jade to collect the great tiger’s body. The mountain-like corpse shrank and vanished, once again astonishing the Salvation Team.

On the road, Lu Yang had the members of the Salvation Team recount their pasts in turn. Lu Yang simply listened, occasionally interrupting with a question or two. After clarifying their doubts, he would let them continue with their stories.

When the last person finished their story, Lu Yang seemed to smile wistfully:

"Each of you had different starting points and experiences, and then you formed the Salvation Team. You were still in sync until the decisive battle, becoming one whole. In the subsequent battle against the King of Mutant Beasts, Shi Lingyun, you made a breakthrough on the spot, defeating the King of Mutant Beasts, and became a hero of the human race. Brilliant, very brilliant."

Lu Yang applauded, seeming to cheer for their life experiences, leaving Zhan Po and the others puzzled. They felt that Mr. Lu was praising them, but the tone seemed off.

Lu Yang took out the great tiger’s corpse in advance and let the Salvation Team carry it as their trophy, allowing them to show off in front of the public.

When they reached the city, the city walls were stained with blood, having endured countless bloody battles.

By now, the news of the Salvation Team’s defeat of the King of Mutant Beasts had spread, and the city gates were wide open, with the excited populace welcoming the heroes back in triumph.

The President came out to meet them in person.

The President was an old man around sixty years old, the former leader of the Top Ten Masters. He warmly embraced Zhan Po and the others.

"Zhan Po, Shi Lingyun, and all of you, I knew you could do it!"

When he came to Lu Yang and met his dark eyes, feeling as if all his secrets were seen through, the President hesitated for a moment before choosing to come forward and shake hands.

"This must be the alien Mr. Lu, thank you so much for saving us."

"This is not a place for an extended conversation. Let’s talk in my office," the President invited the Salvation Team and the alien Mr. Lu to the core area of the city.

In the office, the President personally served tea and water to everyone, showing great people skills.

Lu Yang took the cup of tea from the President, expressed his thanks, and then casually asked, "By the way, Mr. President, what are our surveillance ratings?"

Chapter 1284: Chapter 1283: Isn’t the New Character Unreasonably Strong?

"Ah, Mr. Lu, what are you saying?" The president feigned confusion, pretending not to understand what Lu Yang was talking about.

The Salvation Team and others truly did not understand Lu Yang’s words.

Lu Yang held his teacup, blowing away the steam: "Don’t understand, huh? Then let me change the question. Was the experiment conducted by the mad scientist that created Mutant Beasts thirty years ago really just an accident?"

"Mr. Lu, what do you mean by that?" Shi Lingyun felt that Mr. Lu’s question was bizarre, yet he always felt there was some connection between the two questions.

Lu Yang stood up and paced in front of the Salvation Team: "Lingyun, you come from humble beginnings and rose from the bottom because of your special physique. You have made rapid progress along the way, winning the Beauty’s hand, and though you’ve had troubles, you’ve always resolved them. Do you find your life incredibly thrilling?"

"Zhan Po, as the world’s top expert, you’ve experienced many ups and downs to attain your status today. Silent and reserved but respected by all, I’d imagine your image is quite popular."

"Tianxing, you come from a second-generation influential family but stick to your own convictions..."

"Yuan Xing, you mask your yearning for your wife with laughter..."

"Your stories behind the scenes are truly wonderful."

"Of course, the most wonderful is the director’s design."

...

"Shi Lingyun, having defeated the Weapon Expert, finally became the second-in-command recognized by the Salvation Team. With all members of the Salvation Team assembled, the seven Saviors challenge the King of Mutant Beasts. As for what the outcome will be, stay tuned for tonight’s ’Sky Sea Star Legend’!"

The preview for "Sky Sea Star Legend" played continuously on the big screen.

"Sky Sea Star Legend" is a hit TV series of the Interstellar Alliance, with scenes so realistic that even the most professional special effects experts could find no flaws.

With the impressive acting skills of the actors, unpredictable and tradition-defying plots, and ruthless when it comes to thrilling scenes, it rightfully holds the crown of TV series, consistently keeping a 20 percent viewership rating and a first-place lead.

For the Interstellar Alliance, with its vast array of entertainment options, this is nothing short of a myth.

The drama production is making a killing—just one advertisement slot costs a fortune, and merchandise is in high demand. Each character has their own fan club.

The Salvation Team’s battle against the King of Mutant Beasts is indeed the climax of the series, with conservative estimates predicting viewership could reach 30 percent.

"Who do you think will be the highlight this time? Will the cold-faced sword god Zhan Po make his breakthrough?"

"Hard to say, I think it’s Shi Lingyun. The scene where he absorbs the Enhancer hints that he might fully assimilate it during the battle."

"It might not yet be Shi Lingyun’s shining moment. Some big shot analyzed that the real King of Mutant Beasts is in the ocean—that will be Lingyun’s true opponent!"

Posts about "Sky Sea Star Legend" keep popping up online, the excitement of the audience palpable through the screen.

The director is busily organizing the drama team.

"Are the Nano Cameras adjusted properly?"

"Is the quantum communication channel clear?"

"Can we ensure that Shi Lingyun’s monitoring data is retrieved, so that he can break through during the battle?"

At this moment, the director is ecstatic.

Through "Sky Sea Star Legend," he has already become the undisputed number one director of the Alliance, welcomed wherever he goes, with the financial elite and influential families treating him as an equal.

But he is an artist with aspirations that go beyond this success—he believes tonight will be the pinnacle of his life!

He found the original, undiscovered planet Sky Sea Star, and by inputting everything about it into a quantum computer, he could predict the development of this planet. All he needed was to introduce a few variables based on the quantum computer’s results, and Sky Sea Star would change according to his wishes, making it flawless even in a live broadcast.

To him, money and profits are unimportant. Being labeled as a human trafficker for selling people, or reporting a new planet to the Alliance, he might at best receive an "Alliance Medal," which is so common you wouldn’t know the recipients without actively searching online.

"Sky Sea Star Legend" is different—it is a drama that will make his name immortal, an insurmountable monument in the art world.

Sure, what he’s doing is illegal, but shouldn’t art be unrestricted by law?

"Are we all set? Let’s begin the broadcast!"

With the director’s command, the climax of the drama went live across the net.

Nano Cameras focused on the King of Mutant Beasts, and according to the director’s plan, the sequence was designed to capture the oppressiveness of the King of Mutant Beasts, creating a tense atmosphere like the calm before the storm.

Then, the audience of the whole Alliance saw a traditional Sword Cultivator effortlessly pierce through the King of Mutant Beasts’ forehead, the entire process casually executed.

Director: "?"

Who are you?

The comments section and the bullet chat instantly exploded.

"Who’s this guy, appearing so abruptly!"

"Why is the costume and makeup department so careless, who in the apocalypse is spotless and still wearing ancient attire?"

"Is this a new character, how come there’s no foreshadowing at all?"

"This is the essence of the show, you can never predict what will happen next scene!"

"That kind of makes sense."

"Do you guys think this new character is handsome, like a carefree and casual swordsman?"

"Wait for the spin-off, he must have an exciting past."

From the audience’s comments, this new character was very popular, but the director didn’t think so.

Right now he felt like ants on a hot pan, he was having the quantum computer calculate this person’s actions.

"Hope nothing happens."

Then the Salvation Team and the new character clashed; the new character easily defeated the Salvation Team, and even Shi Lingyun’s breakthrough at the last moment was useless.

The audience could feel the despair and helplessness through the screen.

Later, the misunderstanding was cleared up, nano cameras covered the entire planet; even if Lu Yang flew to the sky, everything was captured clearly.

The Interstellar Alliance audience saw the new character, One Sword Becomes Ten Thousand, annihilated all the Mutant Beasts in one fell swoop.

"This special effect is so realistic, my home quantum computer would smoke trying to render such lifelike effects!"

"This person could probably rival the starfleet."

"Comparing virtual characters to real combat strength again."

"Do you guys think he could be an extraterrestrial visitor?"

"Can’t be, right? Introducing a new map near the end of the show?"

"Isn’t this new character ridiculously strong?"

"I get it, this kind of invincible character is definitely for plot progression, otherwise, there’s no way to continue the story."

The emergence of the new character brought a completely different experience to the audience; the viewership ratings shot up to 40 percent!

The director was in a daze, and the quantum computer only managed to conclude "extraterrestrial visitor" before smoking and giving up.

"Director, what should we do?" The cameraman and others looked at each other, they all signed confidentiality agreements, surely they wouldn’t leak the truth, but how should the story continue now?

The director snapped out of it, now was not the time to sit and accept his fate: "Send a message to the president, ask him to stall this person, gather as much intelligence as we can!"

"The nano cameras are less than one nanometer in size, this person definitely hasn’t noticed us yet!"

The president is part of the production team, all variables on Sky Sea Star are managed by the president.

At this moment, Lu Yang led the Salvation Team back in triumph; the president welcomed them warmly and ushered them into the office.

Just as the director heaved a sigh of relief, putting a cold compress on his face to cool down and plan the next steps, he saw on the big screen that Lu Yang was reviewing the Salvation Team’s past exploits.

"Your behind-the-scenes stories are really fascinating."

"Of course, the most fascinating of all is the director’s design."

Suddenly, Lu Yang turned his head, his face filling the entire big screen, talking to the director through the camera.

"You think so too, right, director?"

The audience was astounded, and the director felt like he had fallen into an ice cave.

Chapter 1285: Chapter 1284: Director’s Jinx

The plot has gone haywire, and the comment section of "Sky Sea Star Legend" was frantically abuzz. Viewers had completely no idea how the TV show’s story was going to unfold next.

Before airing, all those long-winded dissections and analyses of the plot from various experts were deemed useless.

"What’s going on, does this new character know they’re in a TV show?"

"Can some experts come out and analyze this? Has this absurd new character really never appeared before?"

"I dare someone to say ’Sky Sea Star Legend’ is predictable and boring now, like you could guess what’s going to happen next, like it’s either Zhan Po leveling up to deal with the King of Mutant Beasts or Shi Lingyun breaking through to deal with the King of Mutant Beasts!"

Viewers excitedly typed their thoughts; it was just too thrilling, today’s plot was simply too stimulating!

The director and the crew felt as if a bucket of ice water had been poured over them, chilling them to the bone.

"How did he discover the camera!?"

There’s no way the nano cameras could be distinguished by the human eye.

The director, as the main pillar of the team, was the first to calm down: "He must be carrying some kind of scanner that detected the cameras."

"Don’t panic, everyone. He can only talk to us through the camera; he doesn’t know where we are!"

"Even President Ma Jie doesn’t know the location of Sky Sea Star within the Interstellar Alliance, so even if they capture President Ma, it’s useless!"

Hearing this, the crew gradually calmed down, realizing the rationale.

...

"Mr. President, do you have anything you’d like to say, like who’s really behind you, and where they might be?" Lu Yang gulped down his tea, set down the cup, savoring the taste which was mediocre, as was its toxicity.

The faces of the seven members of the Salvation Team went pale; as ten top experts, they weren’t just peak performers in combat but also far smarter than average. Even though Lu Yang hadn’t spelled out the situation, they understood his meaning through just a few words.

The livid expression on the President’s face confirmed their suspicions!

They just couldn’t figure out, if all this was for filming a TV show, then what was real and what was fake?

Were only the seven of them kept in the dark, or was the whole of Sky Sea Star fooled?!

What did everything they had experienced count for, a joke to amuse others?

"President Ma Jie, answer Mr. Lu’s questions!"

President Ma, whose face had been ashen and silent up to now, revealed a smile: "Mr. Lu, you really are an unexpected variable."

He pointed at his mouth with a ferocious expression: "I have a nuclear bomb remote and a locator in my teeth. I advise you to let me go, or once I bite down on the remote trigger, the nuclear bomb will launch right here, and then we’ll all be finished together!"

With the TV show’s secrets exposed, they absolutely couldn’t fall into the other party’s hands. Even if Lu Yang didn’t come after him, the entire population of Sky Sea Star could drown them with their spit alone!

President Ma, as the leader of the previous generation’s top ten experts, wasn’t just a scripted character. He actually had that level of strength, and not even Zhan Po and Shi Lingyun -- who had fully absorbed the Enhancer -- were a match for him.

But he also knew that no matter how strong he was, he couldn’t possibly be a match for Lu Yang, who could single-handedly deal with all of the Mutant Beasts. His only option now was to escape!

He had on him the highest-grade anti-tracking device and a signal jammer, so even if Lu Yang used a scanner, he wouldn’t be able to find him!

The Salvation Team and others were torn; if the nuclear bomb exploded here, everyone in the city would die, but if they simply let President Ma go, it would be hard to swallow!

Just as everyone was conflicted, President Ma dropped two smoke bombs from his cuffs to block everyone’s sight, and amidst the smoke, his laughter could be heard before it disappeared.

Smoke cleared, and everyone saw Lu Yang pin President Ma to the ground, leaving his teeth shattered across the floor.

Lu Yang raised an eyebrow: "Where would I put my face if you ran away?"

"This is impossible!"

President Ma was horrified, when he released the smoke bomb, he also created multiple fake signals. How could Lu Yang possibly find him?

Is their technology level so much higher?

"I can tell you who is backing me; I’m a citizen of the Interstellar Alliance, backed by the Alliance’s TV station. I advise you to release me. Otherwise, when the Interstellar Fleet comes, you’ll be the one to die!"

"Interstellar Alliance?" Lu Yang heard an interesting term, it sounded like a colossal space power, technically probably far superior to that of Sky Sea Star.

It would be great to transplant the Interstellar Alliance’s tech to the Cultivation World, for the benefit of the common people.

But President Ma Jie unwilling to cooperate in the interrogation was a bit troublesome. If he was subjected to a Soul Search, President Ma Jie would become an idiot, which would be too easy on him, and people of Sky Sea Star would have one less target for revenge.

Without a Soul Search, I wouldn’t know the location of the Interstellar Alliance.

Suddenly, Lu Yang noticed the Nano Cameras still filming, he could sense that the Nano Cameras were continuously sending some kind of signal, probably electromagnetic waves or some new term he hadn’t heard of, but that didn’t matter. What mattered was that the other end of the camera was probably connected to the Interstellar Alliance.

He pondered as he pinched one of the cameras, scaring the crew on the other end into a panic.

Soon commonsense prevailed over their emotions, there was no need for them to be afraid. Lu Yang could only talk one way, after all, he had no way to find them.

"Trace Origin."

Lu Yang spoke a word no one else understood, and the Trace Origin Dao Fruit Prototype locked onto the Nano Camera, a line extending to the other end of the stars appeared in front of Lu Yang, visible only to him, not even for Immortal Fairy.

"Indeed, I can find the source of the camera."

Lu Yang found the Trace Origin Dao Fruit Prototype increasingly convenient to use.

Lu Yang kicked President Ma over to the Salvation Team: "This person is up to you. I’m off to visit this so-called Interstellar Alliance."

"Mr. Lu..."

Without even giving time for farewells, Lu Yang excitedly summoned the Black Canopy Boat. Jumping through space onboard, he followed the line extended by the camera toward the Interstellar Alliance.

There was no longer any threat to the Salvation Team on Sky Sea Star, so there was no need to worry about it for the time being. The situation with the Interstellar Alliance was unknown, and any delay could mean the crew escaping, which would be bad.

"What do we do, what do we do, is he coming over?!" The crew was in chaos, completely unable to comprehend Lu Yang’s methods.

Just how far had their technology developed, as if dealing with an immortal?!

The director took charge again: "Don’t panic, you all know how far Sky Sea Star is from the Alliance, and there are countless asteroid belts in between, he won’t fly over so quickly!"

"Let’s call the police quickly, or have the higher-ups deploy the military!"

Being caught by the Alliance government was far better than being seized by a mysterious and unpredictable alien. The director, pulling some strings, knew he wouldn’t face the death penalty, but who knows what would happen if caught by this alien.

"Exactly, an alien attack is like a terrorist attack, no, this is foreign intrusion, let the government protect us!"

Just as everyone was getting ready to contact the outside world for help, a boom was heard overhead, the rooftop was lifted off, and the promotional board of "Sky Sea Star Legend" that had been standing on the roof was placed before them, as a small boat glided down in the moonlight.

An anciently-dressed alien with hands in his robe descended upon the Interstellar Alliance in the Black Canopy Boat.

Chapter 1286: Chapter 1285: Your Servant Will Follow the Decree

Lu Yang was busy searching for the TV drama crew, merely glancing at the Interstellar Alliance, where the crew was located along the way.

Several colossal iron spheres hovered in the air, with one still under construction. Interstellar Spaceships ceaselessly shuttled back and forth, transporting goods. The planet where the crew was located was filled with skyscrapers and radiantly lit up, making it hard to distinguish whether it was day or night.

How could there be such bad people, controlling others’ lives and taking pleasure in it?

This meant that Lu Yang was alone, without support, and certainly would not oppose them or the Alliance for the sake of Sky Sea Star.

The sound engineer’s two arms were actually mechanical arms!

By the time Lu Yang had scanned President Ma Jie with his Spiritual Sense, he noticed that his body was mechanical, and his counter-tracking device and signal simulator were not carried on him, but installed within him.

After finding the crew, Lu Yang discovered that they, too, all had mechanical bodies.

The massive success of "Sky Sea Star Legend" transformed the crew members into tycoons who all modified their bodies.

A comment in the viewer section caught the attention of the onlookers.

Police helicopters circled the building, countless spotlights converged on Lu Yang, illuminating the crime scene.

Crime scene: crew members were dismembered by Lu Yang, the director was beaten the worst, pleading miserably for Lu Yang to spare him.

Bang bang bang—

Countless bullets were fired at Lu Yang, but as they neared him, they all stopped in midair, frozen.

[ Freeze ]

This was the Rule set by Lu Yang.

The pupils of the remote police operators controlling the robots contracted. What kind of technology was this?!

Chapter 1287: Chapter 1286 "My Significant Other

"What is this method?" The bullet lost its kinetic energy in an instant, completely still, leaving both the police and the audience with their jaws dropped.

"His energy shield must have a limit, it can’t stay on forever, fire, keep firing!"

Immediately, the police chief gave the order, which was not his decision alone, as the quantum computer provided the same calculation result.

According to the quantum computer, there was a ninety-five percent probability that the energy barrier surrounding Lu Yang could not be sustained for long; the more bullets congealed, the shorter the duration.

Right after the police chief’s order, they immediately received a higher order: "Superiors have ordered to capture him alive!"

"What?"

Higher-up leaders noticed Lu Yang’s presence, the technology he possessed, and the forces behind him; these were all things the Interstellar Alliance wanted to know, and he absolutely could not die.

But it was too late, the command was given, the rooftop was ablaze with gunfire, hot like a furnace.

Bang bang bang—

The robotic police were covered with gun muzzles, densely packed like a wasp nest, firing different caliber bullets and laser guns, and some weapons that Lu Yang couldn’t identify.

Among the audience were military enthusiasts who recognized that these were the police’s most powerful weapons available; they could collapse a building, let alone hit a person!

Countless attacks came from all sides.

However, regardless of the type of attack, they all congealed at a distance close to Lu Yang, not more not less, just exactly three feet.

Even the exploding shells stopped three feet away, frozen just as they were bursting.

Neither the high-ranking officials of the Interstellar Alliance nor the ordinary audience could believe their eyes, and this could no longer be explained by an energy shield!

Lu Yang waved at the camera, revealing a mysterious smile, and incomprehensible vocabulary flowed from his lips.

He said, "Trace Origin."

Like time reversing, the fired bullets retreated through the barrels back into the magazines, the exploded shells returned to their original form, the opened rooftop closed up, and Lu Yang himself disappeared without a trace, as if nothing had happened.

If the film crew hadn’t disappeared as well.

"What, what is this technology?" The comment section was in an uproar, with viewers continuously posting question marks, but no one could provide a definite answer.

"Is it the theoretical technology of atomic repair?"

"Time reversal, it must be time reversal!"

Immediately, the Alliance’s high command deployed their most advanced warship to chase the Black Canopy Boat, but after the boat performed one Shrinking Ground Into Inches, they could no longer track its whereabouts.

No one noticed that the target they were most eager to find was right under the building.

Disguised, Lu Yang hummed a tune as he left the site of the incident, his clothes transformed into a common style of the Interstellar Alliance, his appearance changed, even his aura was different from before. Even Old Meng, standing here, would not recognize him.

He wasn’t ready to contact the high-ranking officials of the Interstellar Alliance yet.

"Little Yang, what does ’my other half’ mean?" Fairy Eternity’s cheeks flushed slightly, feeling the intimacy of the term, and she couldn’t even look straight at Little Yang now.

"My home is the Spiritual Space, Fairy, you live in my Spiritual Space, naturally, you are my other half." Lu Yang observed Fairy’s reaction with a nonchalant smile, finding it amusing.

"So that’s what it means?" Fairy Eternity suddenly understood, then her eyes lit up, "Then can I call Little Yang that too?"

"No, no need to address me like that." Lu Yang averted his gaze, unwilling to continue the topic.

...

Naturally, the Interstellar Alliance’s high-ranking officials didn’t know that the alien who stirred their nerves tonight was feeling shy.

Twelve projections surrounded a round table, the atmosphere heavy.

Half of them had been woken up from sleep to attend this meeting.

Since the founding of the Alliance, there have been few incidents that elicited such a response from them, and once they had such reactions, the events encountered were inevitably major events that affected the direction of the Alliance.

The last time there was such an atmosphere, it was about resolving the imminent disintegration of the Alliance.

"Has the Ether’s calculation about that extraterrestrial visitor come up yet?" One of them slowly asked; he was the Chairman of the Interstellar Alliance Council, the highest leader of the Interstellar Alliance.

Ether is the Interstellar Alliance’s most advanced and vast quantum computer; the Interstellar Alliance has eight hundred main stars, three thousand auxiliary stars, and a population estimated in trillions. Maintaining such a vast rule largely credits the comprehensive planning by the quantum computer, Ether.

"It can’t calculate specific results, only probabilistic events; the techniques shown by the extraterrestrial named ’Lu Yang’ have never been recorded in ’Ether’," said the Alliance’s chief scientist, known as the greatest brain of the millennium.

Though now only his brain was his own.

"Either Lu Yang is backed by powers that followed a different research path than ours, or their technological level constitutes a generational gap with ours."

"According to Ether, if their technological level far surpassed ours, their influence would have already spread throughout the universe, and the Alliance would not have only encountered them today."

"So does Ether believe this extraterrestrial possesses technology from a different research path?"

"Yes."

Everyone fell into a long silence, pondering the conclusion given by Ether.

"However, if you insist that the extraterrestrial visitor and the records in Ether correspond, there is actually one ’pseudo-record’ that could match," continued the chief scientist.

The other eleven were stunned: "What do you mean by ’pseudo-record’?"

"It means that there are records, but with no supportive text before and after, and present technology can’t verify those matters, like many civilizations’ enlightenment stages containing great floods that end the world or records of immortals traveling through space."

One of them looked puzzled: "You’re saying it might match, you’re not suggesting that the extraterrestrial visitor is an immortal, are you?"

"Exactly."

This time, no one was silent; they directly rejected the conclusion.

"It’s impossible; we don’t need to consider such a probability."

In their eyes, what immortals? Their technology was also perceived as divine intervention by those lesser civilizations.

"Is the greatest probability that it possesses a different research path from us?"

Everyone showed a hint of joy; the Alliance had experienced a technological bottleneck for five hundred years, not to mention significant breakthroughs, there were hardly a few minor ones. Lu Yang’s mastered techniques could surely help them achieve new progress in science!

"What about the issue with Sky Sea Star?"

"What did Ether suggest?"

"Recommend to initiate humanitarian aid and post-disaster reconstruction for Sky Sea Star. Firstly, this follows the longstanding route of the Alliance; secondly, we can start from Sky Sea Star to learn more about Lu Yang."

"Then follow Ether’s suggestion."

"Also, I propose dedicating one percent of Ether’s computing power to analyze Lu Yang’s situation."

"I agree."

"Agreed."

"Agreed."

Chapter 1288: Chapter 1287: A Bustling Library

"Recently, the Interstellar Alliance cracked a major criminal group suspected of crimes against humanity. It is reported that the group, in order to attract attention, disrupted the genetic makeup of alien organisms by disguising a planet as a television program for filming. Currently, the planet has been rescued, and the police are conducting further investigations."

Following that, the Salvation Team, as representatives from Sky Sea Star, visited the Interstellar Alliance and received a warm welcome.

Lu Yang has been at the Interstellar Alliance for five days, and he realized that the streets are filled with promotional posters of the Salvation Team, far more famous than Lu Yang had imagined.

The public, having learned that the "Sky Sea Star Legend" was not a TV series but actual events, became even more enthusiastic about the Salvation Team.

What surprised Lu Yang the most, however, was the emergence of his own fan club.

Although widely revered as a paragon of the Righteous Path while in the Cultivation World, the cultural norm there certainly wouldn’t allow for raising placards and parading through the streets.

The Interstellar Alliance would dare to do so.

Handsome, mysterious, and a champion of justice... These elements combined have made Lu Yang a breakout star of the Alliance.

Whenever Lu Yang thinks about similar events happening on various planets, the corners of his eyes twitch slightly.

While he enjoys the spotlight, the obsession many have with him still scares him a bit.

Discarding his complex thoughts, he walked into the library.

He had been spending his days in the library learning about the history of the Interstellar Alliance.

The history of the Interstellar Alliance, even summarized, would fill an entire row of bookshelves; simply put, it is a melting pot of various planetary civilizations.

Initially, the Interstellar Alliance only consisted of twelve members, but as more life-sustaining planets were discovered, these planets joined the Alliance, eventually forming the massive entity it is today.

However, Lu Yang could not find any records of the Candle Sky Civilization, suggesting that ships from Candle Sky have not reached here yet.

Naturally, there is also nothing about the Blue Star Civilization.

"The technology of the Interstellar Alliance is truly advanced," Lu Yang couldn’t help but remark.

"They manufacture signal simulators for brains; mechanical bodies whose touch sensation can fully transmit to the brain, though this technology is expensive and unaffordable for the common folks."
