"And there are high-speed quantum computers and Ether Computers that can compute anything based on input data."

Immortal Fairy sat on the bed, swaying her little feet left and right, completely oblivious to what Little Yang was impressed by.

The capturing of solar energy is a simple task that the Yaoyang Sect can manage, brain signal simulation is just the Illusionary Realm.

And the Ether Computer that Little Yang kept praising, it sounds rather annoying.

"What’s so great about that? My sharp mind can deduce Dao Fruit, can this Ether Computer do that?"

Immortal Fairy made up her mind; if Little Yang didn’t explain it properly, she’d ignore him for a year... too long... a month... also too long.

Just all day, to annoy him!

"Hee hee, you have good taste, I forgive you."

Lu Yang shook his head helplessly and continued studying the culture of the Interstellar Alliance.

Immortal Fairy disdainfully scoffed, "They’ve only explored so little, at most a corner of the universe."

"Yingtian Immortal and the others could randomly point out someone’s territory, and it would be larger than this area."

"The map is already big enough."

Just this map alone is worth the trip, and coupled with so many technological products from the Interstellar Alliance, it could completely rejuvenate the Cultivation World.

A chip the size of a fingernail fell out from between the pages, and Lu Yang picked it up and examined it under the light. Unable to figure out its purpose, he decided to put the chip back where it was.

Just as this thought surfaced, he heard an explosion not far away, followed by alarm sounds and the panicked voices of civilians.

Lu Yang looked in the direction of the sound and saw a rather luxurious sports car crash into the library, a bloodied young man emerging from it.

Through the gaping hole created by the crash, the outside world appeared in total chaos, seemingly a result of a high-speed chase between the young man and the robot army.

The young man stumbled and ran, gunfire and bullets raining down on him, making it a very dangerous scene.

However, the young man was fortunate; the bullets only scraped by him without hitting.

People from the Interstellar Alliance are not accustomed to reading physical books, and there were scarcely any people in the library; on seeing the danger, they all fled the scene desperately.

Lu Yang felt it necessary to leave the library along with these people.

Not cool, man, why are you coming over here?

Lu Yang thought the young man was so capable, he probably did not need his help, after all, he was just here for a visit.

"Do you want to know why we are being chased? Because my grandfather discovered that Artificial Intelligence wants to topple human rule!"

Lu Yang took out the fingernail-sized chip from the book again and asked, "Is this what you want?"

The young man was overjoyed, took it and compared it for a while, then disappointingly returned it to Lu Yang.

"No, not this one. There should be my grandfather’s mark on the right chip."

The woman had good eyesight; despite the distance and the smoke, she could clearly see what Lu Yang was holding.

Maybe I shouldn’t have come to the library today?

Chapter 1289: Chapter 1288: Melee

The girl’s eyes lit up when she saw the chip in Lu Yang’s hands, but her face turned grave upon noticing the robots gradually regaining their mobility.

"The conglomerate not only sent people to hunt me down but also sent robots after me!"

She felt a sense of foreboding, having not anticipated that the conglomerate would be so thorough as to lay an ambush with robots in this location.

No matter what, I must get my hands on that chip first!

The girl, agile and swift, glanced back at the pursuers, pushed over tables and chairs to block their path, and flipped her way to Lu Yang’s side.

She spoke to Lu Yang earnestly, "I don’t know who you are, but the chip in your hands is incredibly dang..."

Without a word, Lu Yang stuffed the chip into the girl’s hand, a decisiveness that left her momentarily stunned.

Realizing it wasn’t the time to be dazed, she quickly checked the chip.

"Strange, why isn’t it this one?"

She had thought that finding a chip the size of a fingernail in the library meant it was the one left by the contact, but after inspecting it, she realized she was mistaken—It was just a similar-looking chip.

She shook her head disappointment and handed the chip back to Lu Yang, "This isn’t the chip I’m looking for."

So whose chip is it, then?

Among the three people on the scene, only Lu Yang was not in a hurry. The boy and the girl were as anxious as ants on a hot pan. To their left were the operational robots, and to their right were the conglomerate’s mercenaries. There was nowhere to escape.

But they couldn’t afford to flee, as the chip was nearby. Artificial Intelligence and the conglomerate were already aware of its presence here. If they escaped, the chip would fall into someone else’s hands, putting humanity at risk!

They noticed Lu Yang’s calm demeanor, out of place in the chaotic environment, and sighed internally—it seemed that an innocent bystander dragged into this dangerous situation had already given up on thinking.

The robots and mercenaries didn’t dare to make their move lightly, guns pointed at each other, each mistaking the other as the target’s ally.

For a moment, an uneasy standoff filled the air.

"Found it!"

This girl also had pursuers behind her, but unlike before, these were real people.

The new pursuers were shocked to see the robots and mercenaries: "So there are indeed allies!"

Acting first, the new pursuers opened fire, and the robots and mercenaries returned fire, plunging the place into chaos!

Amidst the chaos, the golden-haired, blue-eyed girl dodged bullets and found Lu Yang.

"This chip..."

She spoke with conviction, having escaped the organization with the doctor’s help. Alas, the doctor took a bullet protecting her and died. "I really am not."

Lu Yang wanted to prevent the girl from spilling the beans, but she spoke as fast as a machine gun, explaining the whole situation in a few sentences.

"What, it’s this book!" The boy noticed the book in Lu Yang’s hands, and his body shook with excitement, an idea forming.

"Yes, how could I not think of it? My grandfather’s favorite book was this one; he said that the universe was infinite, and compared to it, the Interstellar Alliance was but a drop in the ocean, completely insignificant. The Interstellar Alliance should hold the universe in awe."

The boy, hugging his grandfather, learned about the mysteries of the universe on the rooftop during his childhood. Just thinking of those moments from his youth made him break down in tears.

Only his grandfather and he knew about this; only he could find the chip his grandfather left behind!

The boy took the cosmic map from the book, pointed to a particular Star Domain, and murmured to himself while turning the pages among the astronomy section’s shelves: "According to the layout, it should be right here."

The first girl noticed the book’s author in Lu Yang’s hands, and her body shook.

"Going to the Supreme Council is very dangerous, I will go alone from here, you guys should not follow me," said Mi Xue’er with a resolute gaze, unwilling to let Lu Yang and the others take risks.

"No, we must go!" Lan Tu said decisively, if the doctor considered Mi Xue’er as his granddaughter, then according to the doctor’s logic, Mi Xue’er would be his sister.

Yu Ran gave a grin: "What are you talking about, how can we abandon a comrade, besides, haven’t we faced enough dangers along the way?"

"They are right, as long as the four of us unite and cooperate, there isn’t a difficulty we can’t overcome, I believe even a Constant Star explosion we would be able to stop!" Lu Yang said with conviction.

Chapter 1294: Chapter 1293 Complicated Relationships

Artificial structures wrapped around half of a Constant Star, endlessly mining its energy, powering the entire Alliance.

For the Interstellar Alliance, this was a common sight, these man-made constructions were the handiwork of the Murong Group.

A youthful-looking person arrived alone at the headquarters of the Murong Group. With a unique identity, he enjoyed unhindered access, making his way to the office of the Murong Family Master.

The Murong Family Master was over sixty years old, yet looked like a man in his thirties. fɾeeweɓnѳveɭ.com

Seeing the youth’s visit, the Murong Family Master stood up with interest, personally welcoming his cooperative partner.

"How is it that the Chairman of the Supreme Council has the time to visit me today?"

The youth took the main seat unceremoniously, snorting coldly: "Subject Number One is lost, I came here to clear my mind."

The Murong Family Master was shocked: "Subject Number One, that’s a serious matter."

"It’s troubling indeed. I’ve eliminated my longstanding adversary, the Star Group, but the crucial evidence chip of illegal Constant Star mining wasn’t found there."

Seeing the Murong Family Master also had his troubles, the youth’s mood considerably improved. He didn’t linger on the two annoying issues and instead shifted his concern to their collaborative project.

The youth stood up and looked up through the window at the Constant Star overhead: "How is the mining of the Sun going, how far are we from the Star Core?"

"Just 6,000 kilometers left, it will be completed in half a month."

Finally hearing some good news, the youth grew somewhat excited: "So in half a month, we will see the full picture of that creature?"

The Murong Family Master’s expression turned strange: "Are you sure it’s a creature? According to my engineers’ speculation, the energy density of that thing is extraordinarily high, not matching any known energy form, what creature could have such energy density?"

"It is definitely a creature!" the youth stated adamantly, "and it’s deeply connected to the corpse I’m researching!"

"You say so, then it is so," shrugged the Murong Family Master. In this field, the youth was the expert, and he did not argue with experts.

"The main thing is that your research can extend my lifespan."

This was the reason for the Murong Family Master’s cooperation with the youth. Although the Murong Family Master’s body was modified to be mechanical, he still felt it wasn’t enough; the lifespan of his brain determined his own, and he wanted to extend it.

And one of the research outcomes of the Supreme Council happened to include this.

The two major organizations thus reached a cooperation agreement, the Murong Family Master would mine the creature from the Sun for the youth, and the youth would extend the Murong Family Master’s lifespan.

After the mining was concluded, the youth would acquire new research materials, which would further extend the Murong Family Master’s life.

The youth sat for a while longer before leaving the Murong Group and returning to the headquarters of the Supreme Council.

...

Lu Yang and his three companions, as guided by the doctor, found the hidden thermal weapons and armed themselves.

Although Lu Yang felt his own clothing was sturdier than the bulletproof vest, out of consideration for Lan Hai and the others’ good intentions, he did not want to disappoint them.

The sports car had limited space, so the four of them could only pick the stronger weapons to bring along.

"We’re not far from the headquarters, time to get off," said Mi Xue’er, directing the sports car to stop on the outskirts of the woods; any further would alert the people at the headquarters.

Lan Hai let the sports car hide itself, while they hid on both sides of the road.

According to Mi Xue’er, trucks would transport goods every day – their opportunity for infiltration.

After waiting for a full hour, a large truck finally approached from the distance.

Mi Xue’er followed behind the truck, extended sharp nails, and cut out a circular door on the truck’s door, signaling the others to climb in. Once inside, she sealed the circular opening with a strong adhesive; anyone looking at it from the outside wouldn’t be able to tell a door had ever been there.

The four hid in the cargo compartment, clenching and relaxing their fists repeatedly, vigilant of their surroundings, attentive to any movement outside the truck. Only Lu Yang was the least conscious of danger, still finding time to chat with Fairy Eternity.

"Mi Xue’er’s Ancient Bloodline concentration seems a bit high, could it be that there are still living Ancient Demon Beasts in the outside world, and Mi Xue’er is their descendant?"

Lu Yang saw it too. His popularity within the Interstellar Alliance was higher than the Salvation Team’s, with merchandise selling at an absurdly fast rate and being perpetually out of stock.

"Oh, then let’s call it merchandise. After all this is settled, why don’t you buy some and take it back?"

Lu Yang felt somewhat embarrassed.

The Immortal Fairy, like a koala, clung onto Lu Yang’s neck, swaying back and forth: "Buy it, buy it, what’s a trip without souvenirs?"

"...But people don’t usually go on a trip to buy their own souvenirs."

Lu Yang, unable to effectively retort, had no choice but to agree to the Immortal Fairy’s insistence.

The large truck carrying everyone passed through the dense forest and drove into the pitch-black cave mouth, stopping twice.

When it stopped for the second time, Mi Xue’er gestured with her hands, signaling that they had arrived inside the headquarters.

The truck and container detached, and mechanical arms arranged the container in another area; wisps of cold air seeped into the box, seemingly being taken to an ice cellar.

After waiting a while, Mi Xue’er, feeling no danger outside, was about to leave when suddenly the container shook, and the walls on all four sides opened simultaneously, revealing Lu Yang and the other three, who had been hiding amidst the cargo.

It was then that they realized they were indeed in an ice cellar, with the container right in the center, surrounded by eight Class A Soldiers, as if they were offering them up as tribute.

Mi Xue’er’s face instantly darkened; she had been outsmarted.

She had never been here, but she had heard the doctor mention that the President of the Supreme Council had discovered a mysterious body, and through studying the body, developed Gene Technology. Her modified genes came from this research.

A rhythmic clapping sound started, and a young man emerged from the darkness, with a seemingly amused look as he watched the surprised crowd.

"Mi Xue’er, does this mean you knew it would be difficult to capture you and you’ve deliberately walked into the trap, or do you think after dealing with more than thirty Harvesters, you’ve become overconfident, thinking you could deal with me?"

"Are you puzzled how I found you? The answer is simple, I secretly planted a tracking device in your body, your doctoral grandfather doesn’t even know about this."

To the youth, Mi Xue’er entering the headquarters via the truck was practically tantamount to walking in broad daylight.

Mi Xue’er aimed her gun at the young man, teeth clenched in anger: "No wonder the Harvester could find us."

Lan Hai, snapping out of his dazed state, suddenly shouted to the youth: "Cycle? Are you Cycle?"

This made Lu Yang very surprised: "You know him?"

Chapter 1295: Chapter 1294: Where is the Power of Bonds?

Facing his friend, Zhou Tian was willing to explain a bit more.

As the president of the Supreme Council, he mastered the highest level of Gene Technology.

But the Anti-Gene Agent stripped her of her power, and she couldn’t even stand up now.

Stand up, I have to stand up and save them!

Their gene technology all originated from research on Mi Xue’er.

Mi Xue’er was so strong simply because her Bloodline was impure, mixed with that of an Ancient Demon.

Facing those Class A Warriors who lay prostrate on the ground, Mi Xue’er chose to ignore them and went straight for Cycle.

The changes in Mi Xue’er completely overturned his understanding; this could be called a Superpower!

This was unscientific!

It was a snow-white rabbit, indistinguishable from pet rabbits seen in the marketplace.

"The Jade Rabbit from Ancient Times," Lu Yang whispered.

Mi Xue’er’s consciousness uncontrollably entered the rabbit’s corpse.

At the moment of entry, thousands of thoughts flooded into her mind—dark, cold, filled with extreme negative emotions.

What is this?

Mi Xue’er felt herself merging with the rabbit, but the rabbit’s negative emotions were also eroding her.

During the process, the Jade Rabbit’s corpse slowly opened its blood-red eyes and merely a wisp of its former presence was enough to crush Cycle’s rib cage piercing his lungs.

No, I cannot be eroded like this, a mere wisp of power killed Cycle, my companions must be in danger as well, if I’m occupied by negative emotions, my companions will undoubtedly die.

Mi Xue’er’s kind consciousness fought against the negative emotions, both sides struggling.

Mi Xue’er looked towards Lu Yang and the others, believing that while she struggled, her companions must also be suffering, their bond could get them through this ordeal.

Then she saw that Lu Yang and the others were completely unaffected by her.

Negative emotions instantly overtook Mi Xue’er’s consciousness.

Chapter 1296: Chapter 1295: The Sun is Going to Explode

Given that Mi Xue’er could withstand the Anti-Gene Agent and awaken her Bloodline, it meant she had incredibly strong willpower; with some effort, she should be able to pull through.

What caused her to suddenly turn evil?

He had merely protected Lan Hai and Yu Ran with a simple gesture, shielding them from the overwhelming pressure, and had done nothing else.

This Jade Rabbit had a strong Cultivation Level before its death, reaching the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, but being controlled by someone like Mi Xue’er who lacked any Cultivation foundation, the power it could exert wasn’t even one ten-thousandth of its potential.

What exactly is happening?

Especially since Brother Meng appeared quite smug, as if he had accomplished something remarkable.

"Your words are so effective, Fairy?" Lu Yang exclaimed, that was almost like Verbal Spell casting.

"That’s right, who do you think I am? Whether it’s a living Demon Beast or a dead one, which one isn’t afraid of me?"

Lu Yang felt that the reason Demon Beasts feared Immortal Fairy was not something worth boasting about.

With that thought, Lu Yang clasped his hands, "His Majesty’s awe spreads far and wide, without dispatching a single soldier, merely with culinary skills, you make countless demons submit—such is the act of a wise ruler."

As a subject, the most important skill is multitasking, thinking while speaking.

"What happened to me?" Mi Xue’er woke up in pain, clutching her head.

It was as if she had turned into a rabbit, charging towards Brother Meng, then she got scared awake?

Lan Hai and Yu Ran hurriedly ran over and helped her up, concerned about her injuries.

"Xue’er, are you okay?"

"I’m fine...I’m surprisingly well, actually." Mi Xue’er had never felt this way before, as though she’d broken through human limits and could effortlessly overturn tanks, her body became impervious to weapons.

What’s going on?

Suddenly, the ground shook, startling everyone.

Didn’t they say it was illegal Sun mining, what the hell did you mine out?

"That mechanical arm looks nice, where did you buy it?"

"Really cool, I might buy a pair when I get my salary."

"Forget it, you think you can just buy it if you want? There’s a queue and a lottery system."

In Sun City, covered with mechanical structures on the Sun’s surface, two engineers from Murong Group chatted casually leaning against the railing.

Despite the name Sun City, there were hardly any people there; operations mainly relied on Artificial Intelligence independently developed by Murong Group.

Artificial Intelligence mining devices automatically extract energy from the Sun and consistently transport the continuous solar power to nearby planets via the space elevator. Engineers here are only to prevent accidents.

Ever since the Murong Group won the bid and built Sun City here, there only occurs a minor fault every thirty years on average, with no major accidents ever happening.

Suddenly, alarms blared from all directions, and red warning lights illuminated the pale faces of two engineers.

Each of the engineers injected themselves with a tranquilizer directly into the brain, forcing themselves to calm down. An alarm of this frequency signified Sun City’s highest level of alert, indicating that more than thirty percent of indicators had spiked.

They hurriedly pulled up the monitoring data, only to discover that fifty percent of the data was exceeding maximum values, and other metrics were rapidly approaching the upper limit!

Sixty percent... Seventy percent...

The current situation was far beyond what the Murong Group had anticipated.

The two engineers exchanged a glance, finding no solace even with the tranquilizer.

"Is the Sun going to explode?!"

But how could this be possible? There have been many instances of illegal harvesting of stellar energy, with accidents occurring in less than one percent of cases, and none of those incidents came close to causing a sun explosion!

The same situation occurred in various Sun Cities. Chaos had overtaken the Murong Group, even the Murong Family Master was unsettled.

The warning from the Star Group was not an exaggeration; the Sun was really about to explode!

Once the Sun explodes, the entire star system would be destroyed instantly, no one would survive!

On the screen, the countdown timer ticked down rapidly, as predicted by the Artificial Intelligence for the Sun’s explosion event.

When the numbers hit zero, the two engineers had ashen faces, but the anticipated solar explosion did not occur.

"Is... is everything okay?"

"Why didn’t it explode?"

"Could it be a system malfunction?"

Just as the pair sighed in relief from the near miss, Sun City shook, the surface of the Sun burbled with bubbles, and a Red Gold feather burst through the energy extraction conduit.

The feather was enormous, even larger than a whale.

A bird’s cry echoed throughout space, shattering countless instrument dials, the high-strength nanomaterials were of no use. freёweɓnovel.com

A pair of Red Gold wings, capable of eclipsing the sky, burst forth with gaps between feathers oozing with magma over ten thousand degrees.

Finally, the two engineers caught sight of the monstrous creature, a gigantic bird with three legs, Red Gold body, and hollow eyes.

The beak contained a never-before-seen ore.

So, the series of anomalies experienced were not the Sun exploding, but rather this Demon Beast emerging from it?!

What kind of creature was this, and had it been living inside the Sun all along?

Before they could revel in relief, they noticed extremely visible cracks appearing on the surface of the Sun, threatening to split open at any moment.

Just being born, this Demon Beast could cause the Sun to crack?!

The giant Demon Beast flapped its wings, and the spattering magma threatened to destroy Sun City!

Just as despair settled on the pair, a figure appeared and, with a punch not clear in features, smashed the giant Demon Beast back into the Sun!

"Fairy, what’s going on with this Golden Crow’s corpse? How come it suddenly started moving?"

"Seems like it was affected by that Jade Rabbit?"

Fairy Eternity pouted, recalling the familiar Golden Crow, when suddenly she realized.

"It must be the research fee paid by Immortal Jiuchong. Since it was unused until death, they probably decided to bury it with themselves."

Chapter 1297: Chapter 1296: 3 Minutes

"I just said how Mi Xue’er could have both the Jade Rabbit Bloodline and the Golden Crow Bloodline, never would have imagined these two species could indeed produce offspring."

Mi Xue’er is indeed a descendant of their offspring.

As Lu Yang spoke, he threw another punch at the Golden Crow trying to crawl out from the Sun.

While the Golden Crow was not a match for Lu Yang in life, how could it be his opponent in death, operating on instinct alone?

With a simple punch, a boundless storm was lifted on the surface of the Sun. Two engineers trembled, unable to escape on their spacecraft, forced to watch the battle.

It was a scene completely beyond their comprehension. The Red Gold colored bird was immense, like a mountain, its emergence enough to cause the Sun to crumble. Its opponent was as small as a grain of rice in front of it, yet this tiny adversary was completely overwhelming the monstrous bird!

What kind of opponent is this, a robot powered by anti-matter energy? Isn’t that just a money-making tech concept? Or some other latest product developed by the Alliance?

Engineers who can work in Sun City are the best in their field, privy to many insider informations, but none match what they’re witnessing now.

This Star System has one Main Star and four auxiliary stars, with a total population of sixteen billion. Everyone is in chaos, even with Artificial Intelligence maintaining order it’s futile, the Sun is on the brink of collapse, the entire Star System is shaking, anyone can see that there’s a major problem with the Sun, not running is waiting for death.

"Stop causing trouble if you’re dead!"

Lu Yang kicked the Golden Crow back into the Sun, but it persisted in crawling out, never-ending.

Moreover, the corpse of the Golden Crow was situated on the Sun’s surface, millions of kilometers from its core. If Lu Yang had to forcefully push it back, he would be exhausted to death.

Lu Yang pointed at the Golden Crow, whispering an order: "Trace Origin."

The Trace Origin Dao Fruit Prototype was activated, and the Golden Crow was moved back to its original position.

Lu Yang followed immediately, arriving at the Sun’s core instantaneously on the Black Canopy Boat.

Seeing that the Golden Crow still showed signs of undying, trying to burrow out of the Sun, Lu Yang had an idea and took out the body of the Jade Rabbit from his Identity Jade.

There still exists the Jade Rabbit Clan within the Cultivation World, and Lu Yang originally planned to return this Ancient Jade Rabbit ancestor to them for a proper burial, hence he stored it in the Identity Jade.

Could it be that the Golden Crow keeps reviving because it’s seeking this Jade Rabbit?

It seemed as if sensing the Jade Rabbit’s aura in close proximity, the restless Golden Crow calmed down.

"Who would have thought that even after the Immortal Jiuchong forced the breeding of the Golden Crow and Jade Rabbit, they could still develop affection."

"It seems only burying them together will let them rest in peace."

The next moment, the Jade Rabbit burst out from Lu Yang’s hands, and the Golden Crow became even more ferocious than before, as if it wanted to come back to life – the two legendary creatures entwined in battle, impossible to separate.

Lu Yang: "..."

So your revival is just to pick a fight with the Jade Rabbit?

What grievances did you two have in life, an uneven division of belongings in a divorce?

He scratched his head; this situation was a bit tricky. Surely he couldn’t chop these two bodies into mincemeat; that would be too disrespectful to the elder predecessors.

"Do you need Immortal to take action?" Fairy Eternity was best at dealing with the dead.

"No need." Lu Yang felt these two elder predecessors had been dead for four hundred thousand years; death hadn’t been easy on them, so there’s no need to scare them with a Fairy now.

Suddenly, a flash of inspiration struck him – he placed the Jade Rabbit within the Green Peak Sword Small World, cutting off its aura; true to predictions, the Golden Crow settled down.

Lu Yang heaved a sigh of relief, it seems his idea was right; so long as he prevented the Golden Crow from sensing the presence of the Jade Rabbit, it would be fine. Previously, he had placed the Jade Rabbit inside his Identity Jade, which is somewhat more powerful than an ordinary Storage Ring, but it still couldn’t completely isolate the aura.

The only thing capable of completely isolating the aura is a spatial realm at the level of a Small World.

Lu Yang flew out from the Sun, noticing that it still swayed precariously as if about to collapse.

With a soft sigh, he stretched out his finger once more, as if performing a Verbal Spell.

"Trace Origin."

The about-to-shatter Sun underwent time reversal, returning to its undamaged state.

Upon flying out from the Sun, Lu Yang saw two engineers who had fainted near Sun City. After examining them, he discovered they had passed out due to the heatwave from the Sun and weren’t seriously harmed; now that the Sun had reverted to normal, they should wake up soon.

With a deep leap, Lu Yang flew back to Supreme Council headquarters.

Yet, unbeknownst to him, the entire process, from his suppressing the Golden Crow to the restoration of the Sun, had been recorded by Nano Cameras.

All of it was transmitted to the Ether Computer database.

Comprehending the essence of the universe? Wang Jinglong wondered, he hadn’t heard such terminology for a long time, it sounded like something only backwards, farming civilizations that believed in nature would say.

"I know what Mr. Wang is thinking, our Cultivation World is indeed quite backwards, so I’d like to request the Alliance to send some people, just like with Sky Sea Star, to help our Cultivation World and provide us with technical support, it wouldn’t be too much trouble, just a few people would suffice."

The members looked at each other, surprised by Lu Yang’s request.

However, Lu Yang’s request was reasonable and his requirements were not high; it was just to send a few people there.

The Alliance certainly wasn’t short on personnel.

"May I ask Mr. Lu, can you tell us where the Cultivation World is located?"

Lu Yang nodded, "This is simple: please, Dean Gao, bring up a star chart."

"Ether, show the star chart."

A comprehensive star chart known to the Alliance appeared before everyone, with the Alliance right at its center.

The star chart was somewhat larger than what Lu Yang had seen in the library, but it still didn’t encompass the location of the Cultivation World.

He had no choice but to mark the location of the Cultivation World outside the star chart: "Roughly, here."

"Mr. Lu, we will need to discuss and decide on this matter," the Dean stated, already having a resolution in mind, but it was inappropriate to make a decision in front of Lu Yang.

"Alright." Lu Yang tactfully exited the Supreme Council.

After Lu Yang left, the Dean closed his eyes and thought for a moment before asking, "What do you all think?"

"I think there’s no problem, he doesn’t seem to be lying," said one of the members.

"No objections," said Wang Jinglong.

"Old Gao, what do you think?"

"Why not ask Ether?" Dean Gao suggested.

"Right, we indeed should consult Ether on this matter."

"Ether, regarding Mr. Lu’s proposal for the Alliance to send aid to the Cultivation World, what do you think?"

Ether quickly provided an answer:

"Send me."

Chapter 1302: Chapter 1301: Your Spacecraft is Too Slow

With the help of Ether, the Supreme Council unsurprisingly passed Lu Yang’s proposal to send professionals to assist the Cultivation World with modernization.

The Interstellar Alliance has its own set of procedures for dispatching personnel to remote areas, not only in the field of technology but also covering aspects such as economics, education, art, and more.

The Interstellar Alliance first planned the round trip, support duration, and various other details, then sent out notifications layer by layer to select volunteers.

Half a month has passed since the start of the process.

Lu Yang knew that the Interstellar Alliance was interested in Spirit Stones and Spiritual Energy, so he made a special gift of a few Top-grade Spirit Stones before his departure.

...

Eternal Star System, Space Port.

The huge silver spacecraft was docked at the Space Port. Its graceful lines and smooth edges, under the dim light, cast soft shadows, as if telling the stories of countless interstellar journeys. People standing below and looking up at the spacecraft felt incredibly insignificant, full of awe and amazement.

"It’s really big." Lu Yang stood underneath the spacecraft, hands in his pockets, and couldn’t help but exclaim. Compared to the spacecraft, his Black Canopy Boat seemed as crude as a broken plank of wood.

This spacecraft was the Star Path, which the support team would take to travel to the Cultivation World.

He received a notification from the Supreme Council that the support team would gather here and head to the Cultivation World. He had come early to visit the Space Port, which he had never seen before.

The Eternal Star System was akin to the capital, and its Space Port was naturally the most advanced of the entire Interstellar Alliance. Larger than many cities, the port handled tens of thousands of spacecrafts daily, docking, resting, and departing through Artificial Wormholes to various Star Systems.

After Lu Yang finished touring the Space Port, the support team took the space elevator to reach the port.

These individuals were outstanding talents meticulously selected by the Interstellar Alliance, famous in their respective fields, and at the very least, each had experience with one support mission.

They carried themselves with a dignified aura, exuding a sense of superiority from head to toe.

For them, going to assist in remote areas was like a chance to bless others with the Alliance’s advanced technologies in all areas.

Once one experienced this feeling, they would undoubtedly yearn to experience it a second time.

Not to mention that the leader of this mission was the notable figure, Dean Gao, the Chief Scientist of the Alliance.

When Lu Yang realized that Dean Gao was leading the team, he was taken aback.

"Why are you here?"

Dean Gao replied seriously, "I’m in self-exile."

"You said our Cultivation World was backward, so heading there counts as self-punishment, right?"

"..."

When Dean Gao volunteered to head to the Cultivation World, the entire Supreme Council was shocked; such an instance of a council member personally partaking in support missions had never happened before, let alone the Chief Scientist like Dean Gao, who controlled the Alliance’s most advanced technologies.

What they didn’t know was that Dean Gao planned to initiate an Ether revolution, primarily because he believed in advancing technology and was convinced that the Cultivation World was far from being as simple as Lu Yang described, and it could indeed promote technological progress.

"Take this." Dean Gao handed Lu Yang a metal box.

"What is this?"

"It’s an Ether Clone. You can consider it a part of Ether that can synchronize with the main Ether through quantum communication."

The metal box was actually the Alliance’s most advanced quantum computer. The screen displayed Ether’s friendly smile: "Mr. Lu, we meet again."

"Can we talk about something? Can you change your expression next time?"

"Ah?"

The support team was surprised to see Lu Yang chatting and laughing with the legendary Dean Gao.

"That’s Lu Yang, right?"

"Yes, that’s him. I heard he’s one of the most powerful people in their Cultivation World."

Although it was rare for those being assisted to communicate as equals with the Interstellar Alliance, considering the way Lu Yang dealt with the film crew, the support team could somewhat understand.

Lu Yang glanced at the spacecraft, "Are we taking this thing there?"

Dean Gao was a bit surprised, "What else? You think we’d use your Black Canopy Boat?"

Dean Gao was thinking practically; a Black Canopy Boat could only fit five or six people. There was no way the support team could rely on the Black Canopy Boat to get to the Cultivation World.

Lu Yang slapped his forehead, realizing his oversight; he had forgotten to tell the Alliance that they didn’t need a spacecraft, as he had a way to take people with him.

"How long does it take to get to the Cultivation World on your spacecraft?"

"About seven to eight years," Dean Gao calculated the time. "By then, we’ll be immersed in nutrient solution to reduce bodily function consumption to a minimum, essentially stopping time."

This was a common method used by the Interstellar Alliance for long voyages.

Just as Dean Gao was about to say something else, Lu Yang suddenly drew the Green Peak Sword, startling Dean Gao who thought Lu Yang was about to attack.

Lu Yang opened up the Green Blade Sword Small World and took the entire spacecraft and the aid team inside.

The relaxed and casual demeanor of the aid team vanished in an instant, replaced by undisguised shock and panic.

"What happened?"

"Where is this place?"

"Did we just travel through?"

One second they were at the Space Port, and the next, they found themselves in an unrealistically beautiful world with lush greenery and clear waters. They rubbed their eyes several times, trying to confirm that the surreal landscape before them truly existed.

It did indeed exist.

"There’s a positioning system on the ship, bring it out and see where we are!"

"Get out all other tools as well, record the data of this place!"

"Dean Gao, where are we?"

Dean Gao was also stunned, he had made ample mental preparations before departing, determined not to panic no matter what.

Yet before they even set off, something he couldn’t understand had already happened?!

Lu Yang jumped into the Green Blade Sword Small World.

Seeing Lu Yang approach, Dean Gao hurriedly asked for an explanation.

"Oh, this place? This is a Small World within my sword," Lu Yang explained casually.

"Small World?" Dean Gao heard this term for the first time.

"It’s a space artificially created by someone. Don’t you know about that?"

Dean Gao’s mouth fell open in amazement. He recognized every word for ’artificially creating space,’ but had no idea what they meant when strung together.

"Why did you bring us here, just to show off your Small World?"

"Your spacecraft is too slow. I’ll use my boat to take you there; it will only take a month."

If it was just Lu Yang himself, he could use the Trace Origin Dao Fruit Prototype to reverse time and return to the Cultivation World, but it wasn’t just about him — there was also the aid team and the Ether Submachine. Therefore, Lu Yang had to resort to sailing back honestly.

"A month?!" Dean Gao’s jaw dropped, the speed was ridiculously fast.

"Can’t I stay out of there? Your boat can fit people, right?" Dean Gao pleaded sheepishly.

Dean Gao was itching badly; last time he boarded the Black Canopy Boat, the journey was too short and by the time he realized, they had already reached the destination. This time, he was determined to study it properly.

"That’s fine."

Dean Gao explained the situation to the aid team to calm them down.

Hearing about Lu Yang’s method, the scientists in the aid team also wished to witness it and wanted to be on the boat. But how could the boat possibly fit so many people? Lu Yang thought of a compromise and opened a window in the Green Blade Sword Small World so that the people inside could see the outside.

Only then did Dean Gao and Lu Yang come into the outside world.

The tower’s navigator called to Star Path: "Star Path, time is up, please leave the port."

"Repeat, Star Path, time is up, please leave the port."

His colleague, with a dazed expression, poked the navigator: "Stop repeating, where’s the Star Path?"

"What do you mean?"

The navigator looked up in confusion, only to see the enormous Star Path had vanished without a trace, leaving only a light boat heading into the vast darkness of space.

Chapter 1303: Chapter 1302: Welcome to the Cultivation World freewebnσvel.cѳm

An inconspicuous little boat is traveling at high speed in the universe, and it is hard to imagine that such a small boat actually carries hundreds of people.

The star domain ahead seems to have been compressed into a thin line; behind, the view is completely invisible; stars on the sides appear to be tilted toward the direction of the spacecraft’s movement. At this moment, it’s as if the black canopy boat has become the center of the universe, with everything revolving around it.

Dean Gao swallows hard, such a scene existed only in theory, which means the black canopy boat has almost reached the speed of light.

In the next moment, without any warning, the black canopy boat disappears and jumps to a position far ahead.

"Space jump technology..."

The last time Dean Gao took a ship from the Eternal Star System to the Sagittarius Star System, he arrived in the blink of an eye and did not see the operation of the black canopy boat. This time the journey is longer, and he can get a good look, yet he can only make out that the black canopy boat can achieve both light-speed travel and spatial jumping.

As for the underlying principles, he couldn’t understand them at all.

The spacecraft of the Interstellar Alliance could theoretically reach the speed of light, but due to material limitations, they could only remain theoretical.

Their most common method for long voyages is to construct artificial wormholes in various star systems and travel through wormholes.

After receiving permission from Lu Yang, two scientists ran out from the Green Blade Sword Small World, taking measurements with some unrecognizable instruments of data they couldn’t understand.

It was their first experience with light-speed flight; every set of data was priceless, and any set could suffice for a doctoral student to graduate several times over.

"May I ask, Mr. Lu, who built this spacecraft?"

"It was constructed by my ancestor and an elder. They just happened to make it recently, one was responsible for making the ship sturdy and the other for making it fly fast."

"Ancestor?" Dean Gao’s heart stirred, typically, someone who could be called an ancestor would be very old by now, and it would be unlikely for them to make any major scientific breakthroughs at such an age.

"How old is Mr. Lu’s ancestor?"

Lu Yang looks up, calculating: "Almost 100,000 years old, I’d say."

It’s true that Ancestor Guiyuan is from 100,000 years ago, but he has spent 80,000 of those years inside the Time Immortal’s little box. Spending one day inside the box meant outside a year would pass, so it’s hard to say exactly how old Ancestor Guiyuan is.

"Cough cough cough—"

Dean Gao suddenly started coughing fiercely, almost collapsing, frightening Lu Yang who quickly grabbed hold of him.

"Are you alright?"

Dean Gao could only cough, unable to speak.

100,000 years, what difference is there from being immortal?!

It’s a good thing Mr. Lu didn’t tell the Supreme Council everything about the Cultivation World. If they knew about this, they’d probably all want to move their families to the Cultivation World.

Does that mean Mr. Lu is also not as young as he appears?

The conversation between Lu Yang and Dean Gao was heard clearly by the support team staying in the Small World.

They looked bewildered, thinking they were experiencing auditory hallucinations due to not acclimatizing to the space environment.

It seems the Cultivation World is not as backward as described by the Alliance...

...

After more than twenty days of travel, the black canopy boat arrives near the Cultivation World.

The trip from the Cultivation World to the Interstellar Alliance took over a month, as Lu Yang was making stops along the way to draw a map of the universe. The return journey didn’t require this much trouble.

Dean Gao stares blankly at the scene before him.

Numerous boats similar to the black canopy boat are navigating the universe; many individuals, without relying on spacesuits and clad in ancient attire, are leisurely moving through space. They greet the people on the boats, drink, and make merry, presumably Cultivators like Lu Yang.

Whether it is those black canopy boats or the Cultivators, upon reaching a certain point in space, they vanish into thin air or new black canopy boats and Cultivators appear out of nowhere in that space.

It’s as if there is an invisible door there, connecting to another space, with people constantly passing through this door to traverse space.

"An artificial wormhole?"

This operation seems very much like an artificial wormhole, but its appearance is completely different from an artificial wormhole.

"Mr. Lu Yang, what is this?"

Lu Yang realizes that a spatial channel has been established, which wasn’t there when he left.

"This must be a passage constructed by another of my ancestors using the embryonic form of a Spatial Dao Fruit."

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord built many space passages near the Cultivation World, to facilitate cultivators in exploring the outside world.

"Space Dao what?"

"The Embryonic Spatial Dao Fruit, you could interpret it as his profound research into space."

Finally returning to the Cultivation World, Lu Yang’s tone even lifted a bit, as he urged the Black Canopy Boat to fly quickly.

Dean Gao vaguely saw something cubical in the distance and couldn’t help but wonder, whose Rubik’s cube was thrown here?

Yet after the Black Canopy Boat made several spatial jumps, the cube grew larger, and its true form entered into sight, casting a shadow over Dean Gao’s stunned face.

The rescue team living in the Small World also witnessed this scene, with expressions of disbelief, they murmured to themselves.

"My heavens, what is this thing?"

"How can such an astronomical object exist in the universe?!"

"A perfect cube; this is unscientific, unscientific indeed!"

At this moment, they forgot all they had learned, utterly astounded by the existence of the cube.

The Ether Submachine habitually calculated the size of the "cube," almost crashing when faced with the result. The knowledge it stored told it that such an object absolutely couldn’t exist in the universe.

But the fact was right there.

What is this cube?

Lu Yang stood at the bow, spreading his arms to introduce it to everyone.

"Ladies and gentlemen, welcome to the Cultivation World."

Is this the Cultivation World mentioned by Lu Yang?!

This completely overturned everyone’s understanding. Previously, they guessed the Cultivation World to be a planet, at most a larger planet with a high gravity coefficient to have nurtured a life form like Lu Yang.

But where is this a planet; any planet, no matter the size, would seem as tiny as dust in the face of the Cultivation World!

Lu Yang piloted the spacecraft to the entrance of the Cultivation World, where the box opened.

Dean Gao saw the planets moving at an astonishingly fast speed through the opening of the box, in complete defiance of natural laws, as planetary orbital speeds could not possibly be this fast.

But only when he got closer did he realize, it was Cultivators pushing the planets!

The rescue team exploded: "Am I seeing things, a single person altering the orbit of a planet?!"

"Is this what Cultivators are?"

"Could these few individuals be stronger than Mr. Lu, the strongest in the Cultivation World?"

"Look at Mr. Lu’s expression; they don’t seem like the strongest to me."

Lu Yang was also curious about these cultivators, especially since they were wearing official attire, "What are you all doing?"

The cultivators recognized Lu Yang and stopped their work, "Ah, it’s Lu Yang."

"The New Year is almost here, and the Dynasty decided to connect the stars to form a few shapes, like the Azure Dragon, Vermilion Bird, White Tiger, Xuan Wu and the like, to make it look nice."

"Who is this person behind you?"

The official cultivators of the Great Xia noticed the differently dressed Dean Gao.

"This is the chief scientist I specially invited from another civilization. Well-versed in both astronomy and geography, he knows a great deal and has come to help with the construction of our Cultivation World."

"So, it’s a grand scientist, welcome, welcome," several official Great Xia cultivators said with a smile.

Dean Gao’s mind wandered, with no response.

Chief scientist?

Knowledgeable in both astronomy and geography?

Understanding a great deal?

What do I know?

Chapter 1304: Chapter 1303: When the Local Natives Think You Are Pitiful

Lu Yang bid farewell to the few official cultivators from Great Xia and steered the small boat into the Cultivation World.

"Are there many...? Well, did you see anyone rowing boats or flying when we were coming here?"

"Everyone you saw can move planets at will."

Dean Gao couldn’t help but take a sharp intake of breath.

The moment he entered the Cultivation World, Dean Gao couldn’t help but shiver a little, as if he had eaten a mint, his mind feeling clearer than usual.

Thinking of the mysterious energy often mentioned by Lu Yang, he asked, "Is this Spiritual Energy?"

Lu Yang laughed: "Do you feel the difference? If you had your original body, you’d feel even more comfortable."

The spaceship zoomed all the way and landed at the Seek Dao Sect’s mountain gate. Taking out the Green Peak Sword, he released the entire support team.

The two junior brothers opened a door in the Sect Protection Array, gesturing for everyone to enter.

Passing through the mountain gate and walking past the bamboo forest, the serene bamboo forest seemed to be the perfect retreat for the reclusive; the river meandered and encircled the bamboo, nourishing it with spiritual water.

Mist rose from the river surface and gradually condensed into a human figure, blocking the way of the group, startling them - what kind of monster was this?

It also felt something strange, something indescribable, and something it had never felt before.

"This is something I brought from the outside world. It’s a Primordial Spirit Clone and might have some connection with you as both are probably Primordial Spirits, and there seems to be some resonance between you."

Primordial Spirits are extraordinarily rare, and the River Spirit had not seen another of its kind.

Of course, that also had to do with its inability to leave the riverbank.

In fact, most Primordial Spirits cannot leave their main bodies; the Ether Computer is an exception.

Now it seemed he had thought too highly of himself.

And this is just a part of the Cultivation World.

Wait, Mr. Lu mentioned that there are few in the Cultivation World more powerful than himself. Just how strong is Mr. Lu?

Dean Gao suddenly realized that what Lu Yang showed in the Interstellar Alliance was just the tip of the iceberg of his true strength!

Entering the core area of the Seek Dao Sect, the support team noticed the disciples fighting on the arena. A brief exchange between two disciples was like a cataclysm, with space itself trembling.

The disciples of the Seek Dao Sect were giving them the kind of look they were familiar with—it was the way they usually looked at indigenous people.

These are mechanical bodies from the Alliance, and we voluntarily modified our bodies. It’s very convenient since any problematic part can simply be replaced."
