"All done?"

To onlookers, it seemed nothing more than Li Haoran giving Old Ji a pat.

Old Ji tried to get up and found that he could move again. The self-diagnosis program also reported no detection of applause.

He moved his arm, stunned.

"What’s wrong?" his companion asked, concerned.

"My arm, not just my arm, but my legs too..." Old Ji said, somewhat incoherently.

Suddenly, he sprang up forcefully, jumping over ten meters high!

The support team’s mouths fell open, and their heads bobbed up and down, following Old Ji’s jumping.

Old Ji’s body wasn’t outfitted with a bouncing function.

"Elder Ji, hold on a second, what’s going on here?"

"I don’t know, I could jump as soon as I got up."

Jump as soon as he got up? When Elder Ji was lying on the ground, what he touched was...

The rescue team looked towards Li Haoran together.

"I just crudely modified his ingenious body material slightly to let him adapt to the environment of the Cultivation World and did a bit of Refining in passing." Li Haoran initially didn’t want to explain, as this kind of thing was just a trivial act for him.

"Can we do the same as Elder Ji?" The rescue team’s eyes lit up; just by briefly touching Elder Ji, his body underwent a dramatic change; what a miraculous skill!

Li Haoran nodded, "Of course, the quality of the material of your mechanical bodies is good; they are just lacking spiritual energy guidance. Give me some time, and I can make you all fly."

"Fly?"

Hearing that they could fly, the rescue team clamored around Li Haoran competing to be first: "Me first, me first."

"I’ll give it a try for you guys."

...

"Dean Gao, this way, please."

Dai Bufan, Lu Yang, and Dean Gao walked out of the Task Hall together.

"So, it can fly without additional devices!"

Although the Interstellar Alliance has bodies capable of free flight, they are extremely costly, far beyond what the rescue team could afford.

Moreover, their bodily functions have been enhanced all around; flying is just one aspect.

It’s hard to believe that simply being touched by Li Haoran a few times could cause such drastic changes to the body.

"I can fly higher than you!"

"Then let’s see who flies higher!"

Dean Gao, seeing the rescue team flying all over the sky, fell into deep thought and remained speechless for a long time.

What happened during the time he was inside?

"Mr. Li, you must be the most incredible scientist in the Cultivation World."

"Mr. Li, such brilliant skills; even our Dean Gao can’t modify us to be like this."

Li Haoran, surrounded and praised by the rescue team, felt somewhat embarrassed; he decided to show the rescue team some real skills.

"Actually, your ingenious bodies can be further modified. If you ask me, keeping the brain is superfluous; just remove the brain and let only the soul attach to this ingenious body; it will be even more comfortable than now!"

The once lively rescue team suddenly fell silent upon hearing this; the method sounded a bit radical...

"Cough!" Dean Gao intentionally coughed loudly, and upon seeing Dean Gao emerge, the rescue team promptly stood in line properly.

"Since you are all guests here, just have fun," Senior Brother Dai tried to smooth things over.

"I apologize to Mr. Dai."

"Junior Brother Li has reached the Body Integration Realm, congratulations." Lu Yang noticed that Li Haoran had safely passed the Void Refinement Stage and become a Combined Great Ability.

Li Haoran clasped his hands together, utterly unwilling to accept Lu Yang’s kindness: "If you don’t boast about your cultivation level in front of me, I’ll be thankful to Heaven and Earth."

Lu Yang laughed heartily and patted Li Haoran’s shoulder: "Junior Brother Li, you’re being too modest. When have I ever boasted to you that I am a Semi-Immortal who can also use two types of Dao Fruit Outlines?"

Li Haoran: "..."

Dai Bufan called for a Flying Boat to take the rescue team and Lu Yang to the Imperial City.

On Great Snow Mountain, Qinghe, who was playing chess with Chasing Moon True Person, sensed something and turned to look towards Sky Gate Mountain.

"What’s the matter, Qing He?"

"It’s strange, I just sensed the aura of Lu Zhuguo?"

Chasing Moon True Person repeatedly shook his head: "Impossible, you must be overthinking it. If Lu Yang had returned to Seek Dao Sect, there’s no way he wouldn’t come to Sky Gate Mountain to find you."

"That’s right, let’s continue the game. Wait, isn’t the position of the chess pieces different from before?"

Chapter 1306: Chapter 1305 Dai Bufan: Praising Too Early

Great Xia, Imperial City, Imperial Palace.

Emperor Xia was reviewing memorials to the throne, with a legal reform proposal regarding cultivators venturing beyond the realm set to his right.

Besides the White Horse Dynasty, the cultivators had discovered several star systems inhabited by sentient beings, with developmental levels similar to that of the White Horse Dynasty.

Several unforeseen issues had arisen during the exploration, and there were gaps to be filled concerning these matters.

Three figures passed through the threshold of the Daming Hall in the sunlight, with Dai Bufan saying loudly, "Your Majesty, we have come to pay our respects."

Emperor Xia looked up, not surprised by Lu Yang’s arrival, as Dai Bufan had already informed him before their departure that Lu Yang was returning with significant gains, and representatives from other major forces would meet in the Daming Hall.

"Is this the person from beyond our domain that Lu Yang has invited back?"

Emperor Xia descended from the steps and ordered a seat to be given, while he noted the peculiar body structure of Dean Gao but did not ask in detail during their first meeting.

"I am Gao Huanyu, Chief Scientist and Dean of the Science Academy of the Interstellar Alliance. It is an honor to meet Your Majesty."

"So it is Daoist Gao, oh no, perhaps it would be more appropriate to address you as Dean Gao. It must have been tough travelling from afar."

"And me, I am called Ether," said the metal box in Lu Yang’s hand.

"And who might this be?" If not for Ether speaking, Emperor Xia would have barely realized it was alive.

"The Ether Computer of the Interstellar Alliance, also a Primordial Spirit," explained Lu Yang.

"Someone bring a chair for this Ether... Daoist Ether."

Soon, a eunuch brought over a chair and placed the Ether Submachine upon it.

"Hurry up and tell me, what exactly is the Interstellar Alliance like?" Emperor Xia noticed the extraordinarily complex structure of the Ether Submachine, far beyond the skill of ordinary people, yet this was paradoxically made by ordinary people, sparking his curiosity.

"It’s a bit difficult to describe directly, Your Majesty, please look here," said Dean Gao.

At that moment, the Ether Submachine projected a virtual star map into the air, displaying the entire universe explored by the Interstellar Alliance.

Dean Gao drew a circle, gesturing to a region: "These star systems are the range of our Interstellar Alliance, with a total of eight hundred Main Stars and three thousand auxiliary stars."

"Our capital is here, on the Eternal Star of the Eternal Star System."

"What are these?" Emperor Xia pointed to the small black dots that kept appearing and disappearing near the Eternal Star.

"Spacecraft, which allow us to navigate through space," Dean Gao indicated for the Ether Submachine to focus on the area where the spacecraft were most concentrated.

The map zoomed in, and soon the projection of the Space Port appeared before Emperor Xia, who viewed the massive structures with great respect for the Interstellar Alliance.

The merchant association could slightly modify the Flying Boats to transform into spacefaring vessels, but that was a method only cultivators could use.

He had heard that the Interstellar Alliance was all ordinary people, and ordinary people were actually capable of venturing into space, a task that must have taken the efforts of many people over dozens of generations.

Then the map’s focus shifted to the Eternal Star, zoomed in, and the streets of the Eternal Star were displayed.

The streets were busy with traffic, teeming with people; skyscrapers lined both sides, and colorful billboards stood on the rooftops, everything was bustling to the extreme, sights never before seen in the Cultivation World.

"Who is he talking to?" Emperor Xia pointed to a pedestrian on the map who seemed to be talking to himself while walking.

"He’s probably conducting business with someone from another star system. This uses quantum communication technology that disregards spatial distance for delay-free conversation," Dean Gao laughed, proud of the invention.

"What about this?" Emperor Xia pointed to the most frequently appearing large metal boxes, which were hanging in the air, similar to the Flying Cars invented by Lu Yang.

But the Interstellar Alliance certainly did not rely on Flying Swords for propulsion.

"Solar-powered vehicles."

"And this?"

"Artificial Intelligence nanny."

"And this?"

"Memory chip factory, fully operated by Artificial Intelligence."

"Ordinary people can live so luxuriously?!" The more Emperor Xia learned about the Interstellar Alliance, the shorter his breath became.

He stood up excitedly and began to pace around the Daming Hall.

The gains brought by Lu Yang were too significant, beyond his expectations.

And this was just the creation of ordinary people; if it could be combined with the Hundred Skills of Cultivation, who knew what heights could be reached.

"Establish the Heavenly Craft Department, we must gather all Artifact Refiners, Array Masters, and Engravers to form the Heavenly Craft Department!"

"Dean Gao, would you consider joining Great Xia’s Heavenly Craft Department?"

"What’s this about joining your Heavenly Craft Department? Let me hear it too." Zhu Tian walked into the Daming Hall with a casual demeanor.

"It seems I’m the first one here, huh?" Zhu Tian grinned, noticing Lu Yang, "Has Big Brother Lu Yang returned?"

He looked around and noticed an empty chair, took the Ether Submachine off it, and sat down himself.

"That’s quite thoughtful, reserving a chair for me."

"Hey hey hey, that’s my chair!" the Ether Submachine protested angrily, wishing it could jump up if not for its physical limitations.

"This little thing can talk, interesting." Zhu Tian chuckled, flicking its ’head’ and making the Ether Submachine spin several times.

"Mr. Lu, he’s bullying me, you have to stand up for me!" the Ether Submachine cried to Lu Yang, startling Zhu Tian.

What’s the background of this little thing, a Primordial Spirit possessed by a metal box?

Lu Yang reminded, "Nation Master Zhu, this is an Ether Computer, a guest who has come from the Interstellar Alliance."

"Oh, a guest, my apologies," Zhu Tian said with a grin and patted the Ether Submachine, "But it’s also your fault, why didn’t you say you were a guest earlier to avoid this?"

The Ether crazily searched its database, thinking about how to verbally counterattack Zhu Tian.

Then Old Dragon Emperor, Snow Emperor, and Ming Yu arrived at Daming Hall successively, and after understanding the situation with the Interstellar Alliance, they too realized it was a rare development opportunity.

Zhu Tian suddenly realized, somewhat indignant, "You Great Xia, where did you get a Heavenly Craft Department from, and even trying to recruit Dean Gao while we were away, Old Jiang, have you no shame, stealing people to your Great Xia first!"

Emperor Xia knew he was in the wrong and remained silent.

Then Zhu Tian quickly changed his tone and praised Lu Yang, "However, it really is thanks to Big Brother Lu Yang that he brought back so much from a single trip. Once digested, it’ll definitely lead to a qualitative leap in the Cultivation World!"

"Yes, yes, thanks to friend Lu Yang," Old Dragon Emperor and the others also generously praised, not just for the sake of Lu Yang’s face, but because they truly felt that way.

How many Cultivators have gone out to explore, and which among them brought back gains comparable to those of Lu Yang?

Dai Bufan chuckled to himself upon hearing this, Junior Brother Lu had finally brought him some pride.

"No good, the Alliance is in danger!"

Suddenly, the Ether Submachine shouted, causing the atmosphere to become serious.

"What happened? What’s going on with the Alliance!" Dean Gao’s expression turned grave, how could the Alliance be in danger?

But the Ether Submachine would not lie; it maintained synchronization with the mainframe through quantum communication technology.

The Ether Submachine then dropped a bombshell, "An unknown force has attacked the Alliance, incredibly powerful, the Alliance stands no chance!"

"Unknown force?"

Dean Gao looked incredulous. The Alliance had been developing, continuously absorbing surrounding civilizations, never encountering such a formidable enemy before. If not for the existence of the Cultivation World, he had always thought the Alliance was the most powerful force in the universe.

Yet now an unknown force had appeared, and the Alliance was completely outclassed.

The Ether Submachine projected the Alliance’s battle situation.

At that moment, the Alliance was a battlefield with incessant gunfire, engaged in fierce star wars. The unknown force’s spacecraft charged through, while Alliance warships crumbled upon contact, completely outmatched.

The Alliance was on the brink of extinction!

Lu Yang’s expression changed; why did the unknown force’s spacecraft look like it was from the Candle Sky Civilization?

Soon, the Ether Submachine confirmed Lu Yang’s speculation, "The unknown force has declared that they come from the Candle Sky Civilization, they are Cosmic Dominators, conquering in the name of Heavenly Emperor."

But right after that, the projection disappeared, and the Ether Submachine no longer responded.

"Dean Gao, what’s going on with the Ether?" Lu Yang asked.

Dean Gao furrowed his brows, "The battle on that end must be too intense, the Ether must have concentrated all its computation power to the mainframe."

Hearing this, Lu Yang slowly stood up, looking around at everyone, "Gentlemen, I believe we should assemble our forces and urgently provide aid to the Interstellar Alliance!"

"That’s right, I agree!" Zhu Tian responded immediately.

"I agree too!" Emperor Xia added right after.

"I agree."

"Agree."

The representatives of the five major forces did not hesitate and agreed to send troops to assist the Interstellar Alliance.

"Gentlemen..." Dean Gao was very touched, not expecting that they would propose to help the Alliance without any hesitation.

Ssszzz—

The Ether Submachine buzzed twice, restoring contact with the mainframe. Its tone was somewhat indescribable, as if hesitating whether or not it should share the news.

"That, uh, it seems, Mr. Lu, you don’t need to provide assistance to our Interstellar Alliance anymore."

"What do you mean?" Lu Yang was puzzled. Wasn’t the Alliance in imminent peril, so how come suddenly, it’s no longer in danger?

"The Candle Sky Civilization discovered the Top-grade Spirit Stones you gifted us and changed their mind. They said they’re coming to subjugate your Cultivation World instead."

Upon hearing this, Dai Bufan quickly clutched his chest and nearly passed out.

He thought this time Lu Yang had become more sensible upon his return and was quite pleased, praising him inwardly, but it turned out the biggest bombshell was waiting for him!

Lu Yang noticed Dai Bufan’s reaction and hurriedly turned to explain:

"Elder Brother Dai, listen to me, I had nothing to do with this, it was just out of politeness that I gave a few Top-grade Spirit Stones, it’s Candle Sky Civilization being too greedy..."

"Elder Brother Dai, wake up!"

Chapter 1307: Chapter 1306: The Difference Between Civilizations

Interstellar Alliance, Sun Chasing Belt.

The Sun Chasing Belt is the outermost perimeter of the Interstellar Alliance’s territory, and can also be considered the Alliance’s first line of defense, where the Sixth and Eighth Warship Armies of the Interstellar Alliance are stationed.

Today is Sunday, and the Warship Army, as usual, is holding a holiday celebration, with only a few people arranged to remain on duty in the watch room. Long stints of interstellar patrol can easily lead to fatigue, making it necessary to hold such events regularly.

Seeing their comrades singing and dancing on the monitor, the on-duty soldier yawned and complained to the person next to him, "Sometimes I wonder what’s the point of our daily patrols in this godforsaken space. Might as well have the Ether Computer take over our patrols."

"Forget it, you wouldn’t say that if you were out of a job."

The person replied nonchalantly, "If I’m out of a job, then I’m out of a job. I can live on government relief, can’t die from that."

Suddenly, a large red exclamation mark appeared on the big screen, and a jarring alarm sounded, "Attention, unknown signal source detected!"

"Attention, unknown signal source detected!"

The two duty soldiers exchanged puzzled looks. In this day and age, there are still unknown signal sources?

Could it be some unknown planet’s space probe that has floated here, with a message like "Let’s be friends" written on it?

But soon, the signal displayed on the radar dashed their fantasy.

The radar screen was plastered with dense signal sources, the numbers flickered and finally fixed at the number one thousand five hundred.

This meant that one thousand five hundred unknown objects were approaching the Sun Chasing Belt.

Their pupils constricted sharply, sensing that something was terribly wrong: "Quick, report to the commander!"

The holiday celebration was swiftly canceled, and the two Warship Armies entered an emergency battle-ready state. The commander brought out the space telescope and finally saw what the unknown signal sources looked like.

"What is... that?"

Rather than spacecraft, it might be more accurate to describe them as giant meatballs, their surfaces wriggling, like one thousand five hundred enormous caterpillars majestically traversing the starry sky.

The commander had seen many civilizations capable of interstellar travel, which eventually joined the Interstellar Alliance.

But none of them had spacecraft as bizarre as the ones before him.

Or is it that these aren’t spacecraft at all, but some kind of interstellar species?

"Report, life system detection has found a large number of life forms inside."

"A large number of life forms?"

"Activate all defense systems, stay alert," the commander ordered, his voice calm and resolute, yet unable to conceal his inner anxiety, "Attempt to establish communication again, we must confirm their intentions!"

Multiple attempts to communicate ended in failure, the unknown fleet seemed to completely ignore any signals sent by the commander, continuing their silent advance.

"Send unmanned ships to block their way, open the energy shields! And report this to the Councilman!"

"Yes!"

In no time at all, hundreds of unmanned ships opened their energy shields, interconnecting to form an energy net, erected to block the unknown fleet.

The commander was fully confident in the energy net; during military drills, he had tested the limits of the energy net, which could withstand the translational motion of a planet for a few minutes before disintegrating—you can imagine the power of the energy net.

However, this net crumbled at the mere touch of the unknown fleet, proving utterly inadequate as a barrier.

"How is this possible!" The soldiers were dumbfounded at the sight, it was utterly unbelievable.

The commander finally determined that the newcomers were hostile and decisively gave the order: "All units, attack!"

Laser guns, particle beams, and missiles shot at the enemy like rain, instantly illuminating the pitch-black space.

...

"Sixth Legion, respond immediately if you hear this!"

"Eighth Legion, respond immediately if you hear this!"

The Councilman kept calling out to the fleets to no avail, beads of sweat forming on his brow in desperation.

"Ether, bring up the Sun Chasing Belt’s surveillance for me!"

However, before Ether could comply, the screen lit up, and on the other end was not any commander.

"So, this is how you operate it, huh? Let me see, there we go."

A humanoid life form stood on the other side of the screen, dressed impeccably, looking quite distinguished.

"Who are you, and where are the Sixth and Eighth Legions!"

"The Sixth and Eighth Legions? Oh, you mean those not very friendly little toys that greeted me?" The humanoid life form spoke relaxedly, snapped his fingers, and the camera cut to space.

The ships from the Sixth and Eighth were being devoured by the writhing flesh walls of the unknown fleet, leaving only half of their hulls intact.

Seeing this, the Councilman’s head felt like it had been struck by a hammer, dizzy and throbbing.

How long had it been since he lost contact with the two fleets, and they had already been annihilated?

Just how powerful was the enemy?!

The camera switched again, this time showing the interior of the unknown fleet, which looked like the inside of a biological body, with the legion commanders devoured by the walls, leaving only their heads.

"Chong En!" the Councilman called out the Commander’s name.

The camera switched to the humanoid life form as a mocking smile curled at the corner of his mouth, "Don’t worry, we simply wish to extract the language of communication with you from his brain."

Only then did the Councilman realize that the humanoid life form had been speaking Alliance language all along.

"What exactly are you people!"

"Us? We are the Cosmic Dominator of the Candle Sky Civilization, under the command of Emperor Fengtian to subjugate all directions. It just so happens that we stumbled upon you."

"As for me, I am the Commander of the Biluo Sky Fleet, Shi Wumian."

"If the Interstellar Alliance is willing to submit to our Candle Sky Civilization and become our vassal, bowing in submission and regularly presenting tributes, you can be spared the scourge of war, how about it?"

The Councilman erupted in anger, "Daydreaming, the Interstellar Alliance will never bow before any power!"

Shi Wumian sighed, "Every conquest encounters the same rhetoric, but isn’t the end result always the same?"

He turned and ordered the Biluo Sky Fleet, "All units prepare, jump to the Eternal Star System!"

...

The Councilman’s expression was as grim as still water. The Candle Sky Civilization was both malevolent and extraordinarily powerful. Two entire Warship Armies of the Candle Sky Civilization could not last more than ten minutes. Even if all the remaining Warship Armies were called back, they would most likely still be no match for the Candle Sky Civilization.

The only plan for now was...

"Ether, all twelve Warship Armies of the Interstellar Alliance are under your control, do your utmost to stop the Candle Sky Civilization invasion!"

The Councilman had always distrusted Artificial Intelligence, feeling secure only when the army was in his own hands. But with the imminent threat, relying solely on his command was impossible to defeat the Candle Sky Civilization; only with Ether controlling the entire army would there be a chance to fight against the Candle Sky Civilization!

...

After the Biluo Sky Fleet jumped to the outskirts of the Eternal Star System, they were immediately met with military interception.

However, the strength of the Candle Sky Civilization was far beyond the Councilman’s expectations. They charged through the Eternal Star System unbridled, invulnerable to any attack, and completely unaffected.

In the face of absolute power, no tactics could bridge the gap.

Such a large-scale battle could not be concealed from the public, and the Ether Computer could not spare the computing power to manage the online discourse.

The people wailed, their once invincible fleet was no more than oversized ants before the Candle Sky Civilization.

"Maybe we should just surrender, being under the powerful Candle Sky Civilization wouldn’t be so bad."

"Yeah, surrendering doesn’t mean a loss, Candle Sky Civilization might even help the Alliance develop."

"Disgusting, spineless, without any bottom line."

"Traitors should die, the Alliance will never surrender!"

Although many people would rather die than surrender, there was an equally significant number advocating for surrender; in their view, this was a completely meaningless war.

"If we don’t surrender, what can we do? Is there anything left to fight with?"

"There is, don’t forget we still haven’t used our Star Annihilation Cannon yet."

"Yes, we still have the Star Annihilation Cannon."

The words "Star Annihilation Cannon" reignited confidence within the Interstellar Alliance. This was their ultimate weapon, capable of unleashing an energy beam powerful enough to destroy a planet in an instant, its sheer might terrifying to all.

Ether Computer lured the Candle Sky Civilization into an ambush and decided to employ the concealed Star Annihilation Cannon.

The stored Anti-Matter met with matter and annihilated rapidly, unleashing a huge crystalline blue energy mass. Under the binding of a magnetic field, the energy converged into a beam, aiming at the command ship where Shi Wumian was located.

As the energy beam of the Star Annihilation Cannon blasted forth, a dazzling brilliance enveloped the entire warship, as if a new star had been born in space.

Everyone held their breath, waiting for the outcome.

As the light gradually faded, the command ship still hovered stably in place, its hull breached with a large, charred hole.

But quickly, the hole sprouted flesh, sealing the breach.

Witnessing this, the Councilman felt as if he had fallen into an abyss, slumped in his chair, his gaze empty and utterly desperate.

It was over, all was lost; even the Star Annihilation Cannon was ineffective. What could the Interstellar Alliance possibly bring forth to combat the Candle Sky Civilization?

"Annihilation Star Weapon, huh? Well, it’s not surprising that the Interstellar Alliance has developed such a weapon, given their level of advancement."

Shi Wumian spoke coldly; they too possessed Annihilation Star Weapons, once considered ultimate weapons.

Since Lord Heavenly Emperor ascended to power, the Candle Sky Civilization had advanced further, and Annihilation Star Weapons were merely powerful weapons.

"Thank the Lord Heavenly Emperor."

If it had been the Candle Sky Civilization of the past, facing the Interstellar Alliance would mean victory, but not an easy one.

Zero casualties in the battle; such an outcome only occurs when there is a disparity between civilizations.

The Biluo Sky Fleet blockaded the Eternal Star System, with Shi Wumian piloting the command ship down to Eternal Star.

Suddenly, several incredibly bright spots appeared on the command ship’s Spirit Stone radar. Normally unflappable, Shi Wumian’s heart skipped a few beats upon seeing these points.

"Does this planet possess the Top-grade Spirit Stones that Lord Heavenly Emperor needs?!"

Chapter 1308: Chapter 1307: The End of Heavenly Emperor’s Good Days

Before each departure, the Ninth Layer Heaven Fleet not only carries the mission to campaign in all directions and propagate the greatness of Lord Heavenly Emperor, but also harbors a covert task—seeking Spirit Stones.

The Candle Sky Civilization had its roots in the mining of Spirit Stone veins, harnessing the Spiritual Energy within these stones to enhance organic bodies, thus creating formidable battleships and unrivaled Candle Sky Soldiers.

After the rule of Lord Heavenly Emperor over the Candle Sky Civilization, the utilization of Spirit Stones reached a whole new level!

It could be said that Spirit Stones are of utmost importance, both for Lord Heavenly Emperor and for the Candle Sky Civilization.

Although each battleship was equipped with a Spirit Stone detection radar, and they had been searching for a long time, they found nothing beyond the birthplace of Lord Heavenly Emperor.

At last, they had found Spirit Stones.

And not just any, but Top-grade Spirit Stones!

If fortunate enough to find a vein of Top-grade Spirit Stones, Lord Heavenly Emperor would surely reward them, and the Biluo Sky Army would inevitably become the premier force in the Ninth Layer Heaven!

Originally, Mr. Shi planned to meet with the Councilman to bring him into submission, but now with Top-grade Spirit Stones before him, everything else had to wait!

After disembarking, he rushed to the Science Academy laboratory at breakneck speed based on the radar directions, his personal guards struggling to keep up.

A few scientists were inspecting the energy contained within the Top-grade Spirit Stones using various instruments, completely unaware of the outside world, when Mr. Shi kicked open the heavy alloy doors, startling them.

Mr. Shi had no time to bother about the scientists’ reactions, his gaze intently fixed on the several Top-grade Spirit Stones under the glass cover, his breathing growing heavier.

There was no mistake, these were Top-grade Spirit Stones!

He smashed the glass cover with a punch and took the Top-grade Spirit Stones.

"Mr. Shi."

Mr. Shi’s guard, arriving belatedly and breathless from trying to keep pace, promptly caught up.

"I have a task for you, quickly investigate the origin of these Top-grade Spirit Stones."

"Yes!"

After speaking, Mr. Shi, holding the Top-grade Spirit Stones, returned to the command ship to wait for the news from his guard.

His personal guards were all exceptional Candle Sky Soldiers, remarkable in martial prowess and reliable in their duties.

"Mr. Shi, this is a list of defectors from the upper echelons of the Interstellar Alliance, please peruse."

"Put it over there."

"Sir, this is the territorial extent of the Interstellar Alliance."

"Put it there."

"Boss, this is about the technological advances of the Interstellar Alliance. I think what we need to focus on most are the Ether Computer and the quantum communication technology. Both technologies are unavailable to us, especially the quantum communication that allows real-time communication regardless of distance..."

"Put it over there."

The Biluo Sky Army had waged wars across numerous planets, and department heads each took charge of their tasks; according to regulations, they would submit the found intelligence to Mr. Shi, facilitating his strategy planning.

The Interstellar Alliance represented the highest level of civilization the Biluo Sky Army had encountered; normally, Mr. Shi would eagerly examine such intelligence upon receiving it.

But now, Mr. Shi only felt impatient; the Interstellar Alliance wasn’t going anywhere after all, these matters seemed trivial. What mattered most was the origin of these Top-grade Spirit Stones.

Finally, his guard returned with critical intelligence.

"Sir, we have clarified that these Top-grade Spirit Stones do not belong to the Interstellar Alliance, but come from a place called the Cultivation World."

"The Cultivation World?" Mr. Shi frowned, having never heard of this place.

"Explain in detail."

"It starts with a Cultivator named Lu Yang who accidentally entered a television program..."

Hearing this, Mr. Shi clasped his hands over his mouth, frowning in deep thought.

"You’re saying that the Cultivation World has a large amount of Top-grade Spirit Stones and is considerably backward, just stepping into the cosmos, and still requires assistance from the Interstellar Alliance?"

Mr. Shi’s eyes gleamed as the phrase "the Cultivation World has a large amount of Top-grade Spirit Stones" continuously revolved in his mind. freewebnovel.com

A backward civilization with advanced energy, is it not like a child holding gold in a busy market? It’s just waiting to be robbed!

The guard nodded: "Yes, it’s strange. It seems that as soon as they stepped into the cosmos, they could traverse wormholes to reach the Interstellar Alliance."

Mr. Shi waved his hand: "Read more books; it’s just a technological explosion, a very normal occurrence. Before Lord Heavenly Emperor emerged, our Candle Sky Civilization, in order to maintain our rule, continuously suppressed and dominated discovered civilizations, precisely because we feared other civilizations undergoing a technological explosion that could shake our position."

"I presume this Cultivation World has found a way to utilize Spirit Stones, allowing for their civilization to rapidly develop."

"But no matter how fast they develop, how can they be faster than our fleet’s speed?"

The guard exclaimed shocked: "You mean... we go to the Cultivation World now?"

"Of course, compared to the Cultivation World, what is this Interstellar Alliance? Have you figured out the location of the Cultivation World?"

"The person named Lu Yang left behind a star map from the Interstellar Alliance to Cultivation World. Please have a look." The guard offered the map with both hands.

Upon seeing this, Mr. Shi burst into hearty laughter: "Great, great, great, this Lu Yang really does only good deeds, he leaves behind exactly what I need!"

"But this Lu Yang seems very capable. He managed to cover the whole planet with Sword Array, eliminating all the Fierce Beasts, and even made bullets stop and return to their magazines," the guard said softly, with lack of confidence.

"What’s that? It’s just some clever tricks, nothing but instantly killing all animals. Any of our warships’ self-targeting cannons can manage that."

"And such warships, we have fifteen hundred of them."

"As for minor skills like stopping bullets, I want to see what those skills can do against the fully organized Biluo Sky Army!"

"This Lu Yang says he is one of the strongest in the Cultivation World, doesn’t he? Then the Cultivation World is just so-so!"

"Pass the word, prepare to conquer the Cultivation World!"

"And yes, routinely report the progress to Lord Heavenly Emperor. Go write down today’s events and send someone with the letter."

"Yes."

...

Candle Sky Civilization.

The Heavenly Emperor resides atop a nine-layer tower.

Once he was Emperor Wu Yao of Yu, and now he is the Heavenly Emperor reigning over the cosmos. His aura has become increasingly profound and inscrutable. It’s less apt to say he is the leader of the Candle Sky Civilization, and more fitting to say he is its deity.

"Your Majesty, a letter from the Biluo Sky Army." A beautiful maid approached cautiously with a letter in her hand.

Even though she had served beside the Heavenly Emperor for several months, she still felt the overwhelming imperial authority of the Heavenly Emperor, deep and unfathomable, being extremely careful with every action, fearing to commit any taboo.

"Is it a letter from Mr. Shi?" The Heavenly Emperor opened his eyes, his pupils reflecting the stars.

He took the letter, and seeing the maid still being so cautious, he couldn’t help but give a wistful laugh: "Cui’er, I’ve told you, there is no need to be so cautious around me."

The maid named Cui’er didn’t dare to defy the Heavenly Emperor, and only managed a soft: "Yes."

The Heavenly Emperor shook his head helplessly, opened the envelope, and quickly began reading.

"Oh, Mr. Shi has discovered a cosmic force called the Interstellar Alliance, and also found clues to the Top-grade Spirit Stones."

The Heavenly Emperor laughed, this was indeed excellent news.

After so many years, we finally found a second planet with Spirit Stones.

"Mr. Shi has already led the Biluo Sky Army toward there, the destination is called... the Cultivation World?!"

The Heavenly Emperor suddenly stood up, staring intently at the word "Cultivation World," his eyes blood-red, his lips trembling.

Mr. Shi, you’re not my subordinate, you’re my father!!!

Chapter 1309: Chapter 1308: How Could I Not Know There Are Many Spirit Stones in the Cultivation World?

"Where is Shi Wumian? Get him back here immediately!" The Heavenly Emperor’s eyes darkened; this was a matter of life and death.

Can I not know that the Cultivation World has Spirit Stones? Is it that I don’t want to mine them in the Cultivation World?

Maid Cui’er was somewhat confused. In her memory, His Majesty the Heavenly Emperor always had absolute power and everything under control. How could he be so impatient?

"Your Majesty, General Shi’s legion is a million light-years away from here, and we cannot notify him directly."

After the maid mentioned this, the Heavenly Emperor remembered that his communication with Shi Wumian was delayed. By the time the message reached him, the Biluo Sky Army would have already embarked on their military expedition to the Cultivation World... Bah, can that even be called a military expedition? That’s marching to their doom!

No one knew the terrifying aspects of the Cultivation World better than the Heavenly Emperor.

"Today is simply the recurrence of those Great World Struggles from those eras."

"Opening the Cultivation World is in accordance with the trend, a move to comply with heavenly fate. Although that so-called Cosmic Dominator is not a worry, the common people are ignorant of the Cultivation World’s strength."

"As all things divide into yin and yang, this event is also a good thing. The Cultivation World has been peaceful for too long, lacking external pressure. The emergence of the Candle Sky Civilization provides ample pressure, helping them achieve their breakthroughs."

Lu Yang’s eyelid twitched, Gu Junye’s set of theories was indeed quite intimidating.

In secret, a pair of dark eyes settled on Gu Junye.

The hidden mastermind watched Gu Junye with a mixture of surprise and doubt, trying to see through him.

Logically, there should be some influence from a previous life after reincarnation. Although what Gu Junye said wasn’t entirely correct, he did touch on some ancient secrets hidden within history, secrets that no one had told him about.

"Could it be that he is the reincarnation of the person I possessed?"

Chapter 1313: Chapter 1312: The Lame Trick

After finishing a day’s work, Gu Junye returned to his abode.

The dim candlelight flickered faintly, barely illuminating the entire abode. A pond was constructed in the center of it, where a pool of lotuses was planted. His calligraphy adorned the walls, imparting a primitive and imposing air. Next to it stood a bookshelf, displaying ancient tomes.

The entire abode was antique and elegant, reminiscent of styles from ancient times yet distinct, designed by Gu Junye himself.

He took off his shoes and stepped into the lotus pond, sitting cross-legged on a green lotus leaf. As the lotus bloomed, a soft halo radiated around him, making his presence enigmatic and profound.

This was Gu Junye’s daily routine for cultivation. Although the newspaper office was known as a holy land for worldly cultivation, merely delving into the mundane world was not enough; cultivation was also necessary.

One flower represents a world; one leaf, a state of Buddha. Gu Junye, sitting on the green lotus, closed his eyes. At this moment, he didn’t feel like he was sitting on a lotus, but rather dwelling at the supreme heights of myriad realms. Each flower, each drop of water represented a world; the myriad realms revolved around him. His fate and the cultivation world were closely intertwined, the stronger he became, the stronger the cultivation world would become.

An unheralded dark figure appeared in the abode, frowning at Gu Junye who was in the midst of cultivation.

The mastermind behind the scenes observed for a long time, still uncertain if Gu Junye was the person he was looking for.

He had barely escaped death by feigning it. Everything had settled down, the cultivation world had opened, and everyone was in harmony, joyful together. If he acted rashly, he might disturb this peace and tangle again with the Immortal Fairy and Yun Zhi, causing trouble.

He wasn’t fond of provoking issues. Had he known that dealing with the Immortal Fairy would bring so much trouble after her death, he would have chosen a different method to tackle her.

Thus, unless necessary, he would not take action.

But Gu Junye’s identity was still uncertain to him; this uncertainty was a vulnerability that needed his own investigation.

"Boy, do you know who I am?"

It was supposed to be only Gu Junye in the abode, but suddenly a stranger’s voice emerged. Anyone would panic in such a situation, only the degree would vary. However, Gu Junye remained unfazed.

He slowly opened his eyes, seeing the dark figure, whose identity was unknown, and said calmly:

"You’ve finally arrived."

The shadowy figure was instantly shocked. Was it really him?

Hearing the tone, had he recovered all his memories? How could this be possible given his current cultivation level? Could it be that the effect of the Reincarnation Dao Fruit Prototype differed from his estimation?

Immediately turning his surprise into joy, it seemed Gu Junye’s identity was almost certainly confirmed. He could deal with it directly, but to be safe, further confirmation was needed.

"Do you know who I am?"

Gu Junye let out a light laugh, as if mocking the shadowy figure for asking a foolish question.

"You have your answer, don’t you?"

The shadowy figure’s breath hitched, Gu Junye had hit the nail on the head, Gu Junye’s composed demeanor was only possible for a reincarnator who had retrieved memories from a previous life.

He had actually already confirmed Gu Junye’s identity.

Gu Junye formed a lotus gesture with one hand, a mysterious smile hovering on his lips, akin to Buddha smiling at a flower: "I thought that by undergoing reincarnation, I could sever causality and start anew. But it seems the causality between us is too deep, and it cannot be severed even through cycles of reincarnation."

Gu Junye looked at the shadowy figure, sighing deeply: "Ah, so focused on causality, how can you advance further?"

The shadowy figure’s heartbeat slowed, astonished by Gu Junye’s words—it seemed he knew more than the shadowy figure had assumed.

As he spoke, did it imply he wanted to voluntarily sever ties and causality with him? "Do you mean you won’t expose my identity, and you do not mind that I possessed you?"

Gu Junye heard this and burst into laughter, tears streaming down: "Possessed? Merely trapped by the shell of my past life!"

"You have trapped yourself here, unable to extricate yourself and have already been punished; why should I bother with you anymore?"

The mastermind behind the scenes trembled, not expecting such an understanding of possession, and upon reflection, what Gu Junye said made a lot of sense.

Could it be that he, having undergone nine cycles of reincarnation, has reached an unknowable state of enlightenment?

If he were to put himself in Gu Junye’s shoes, with his position and cultivation level, could he remain as unflustered if roles were reversed?

The answer is no; his mindset entirely depends on his cultivation level.

The mastermind behind the scenes felt deeply ashamed and couldn’t lift his head in front of Gu Junye.

In terms of cultivation level, he was many levels higher than Gu Junye, but when comparing mind states, he was inferior; Gu Junye was far beyond him.

The mastermind behind the scenes deeply envied Gu Junye’s state of mind, this state of boundless freedom and ease, unconstrained by cultivation level—isn’t this what he had been pursuing all his life?

How could he attain such a state of mind? Perhaps it requires acquiring the Recarnation Dao Fruit Prototype and undergoing nine lifetimes of reincarnation, achieving consummation of the Dao Fruit and developing the mind state naturally? ƒгeewebnovёl.com

Does that mean he needs to die nine times?

Seeing the mastermind in deep thought, Gu Junye knew what he was contemplating: "If you are free, why not meet with Xuanyuan Sword Master? He is now blocked by the barrier from his past knowledge and refuses to stir up past memories. You had a good relationship with him in a past life; maybe your appearance could help complete his cultivation."

The mastermind was stunned; what did that mean?

"Hold on, who do you think I am?"

"Your beloved bestowed her heart to me and rejected your love. In a critical moment, she took a fatal blow for me and passed away unexpectedly. Although it was an accident no one wished for, you always felt the fault lay with me. You took advantage of my tribulation to launch a sneak attack and try to possess my weak body."

"Netherworld Venerable, I didn’t want to bring this up; why must you ask?"

The mastermind behind the scenes: "..."

No, who the hell is the Netherworld Venerable?!

What is all this about!

The mastermind behind the scenes realized he had been completely fooled by Gu Junye and was terribly tricked.

He stared at Gu Junye fiercely, emitting a ghastly aura, causing the entire abode space to tremble.

The mastermind gasped heavily, face twisted ferociously, debating whether or not to simply kill Gu Junye.

"Boy, you did well!" those five words squeezed through his teeth, as a deathly aura unprecedentedly neared Gu Junye.

While killing Gu Junye would be easy, doing so would also expose the fact that he was still alive, rendering all his efforts in vain.

His hands clenched tightly, creaking, and he ultimately decided to let Gu Junye go.

Now, he just wanted to slap himself; damn it, why did he have to come here and suffer? Wouldn’t it be better to stay by Lu Yang’s side and enjoy himself?

The mastermind couldn’t wait to leave this place; with a cold snort, he disappeared as if he had never been here.

Gu Junye still maintained his seated lotus position, his eyes puzzled and particularly confused.

"Strange, wasn’t I in the middle of cultivation, why did I stop and open my eyes?"

"That’s right, it must be because my mind state has yet to reach perfection; I need to continue my cultivation."

He closed his eyes again, quickly entering a meditative trance, immersing himself in a world contained within a single bloom.

Chapter 1314: Chapter 1313: The Fleet Descends, Peril Comes to the Cultivation World!

The Cultivation World had been in a state of war preparation for over half a year, and news of cultivators making breakthroughs followed in quick succession. "mini Lu Yangs" and talents comparable to Lu Yang were springing up everywhere, as if every genius could compete with the famous Lu Yang of the past in arm wrestling.

The so-called "Little Meng Jingzhous" were much fewer in number, as mimicking Meng Jingzhou was a daunting challenge—that every genius didn’t dream of spending a spring night with a Holy Daughter or a Demoness.

Initially, Lu Yang wanted to stop this negative trend, but given his previous fame and everyone taking him as their target, the bad influence was overwhelming and simply unstoppable.

Lu Yang could only sigh about this. Spending his days in the newspaper office reading intelligence reports, after some time, he automatically filtered out the words "mini Lu Yang."

This also reflected the vibrant and aspirational spirit of the current Cultivation World. Everyone was seizing this great opportunity and cultivating as if their lives depended on it.

If one could distinguish themselves in the upcoming battle against the Candle Sky Civilization, that would be perfect.

By now, enough events were unfolding in the Cultivation World every moment to fill the newspapers, and the weekly publications were no longer satisfying the needs of the populace.

Fortunately, Dean Gao’s rescue team had achieved a significant breakthrough in the integration of spiritual energy and technology, making it possible to mass-produce Quantum Communication Devices. However, the cost had not yet come down, so it was common for several households to pool their resources to purchase a single device.

Communication efficiency improved significantly, and it was only logical for newspapers to go from "Cultivation Weekly" to "Cultivation Daily."

"How strange, why haven’t the Candle Sky Civilization’s warships arrived yet?" Emperor Xia and others were puzzled. It had already been over half a year, and Lu Yang took less than a month to return to the Cultivation World from the Interstellar Alliance.

"Could they have encountered some mishap on the way?" Zhu Tian speculated while chatting with Emperor Xia using a Quantum Communication Device.

"Aren’t they supposed to be Cosmic Dominators? What kind of mishap could there be?"

...

The launch of "Cultivation Daily" meant publishing a newspaper every day, which significantly increased the workload. Lu Yang really couldn’t handle it and wanted to sneak away.

But after all, it was he who had told Daoist Xiantian and Gu Junye that he would handle the newspaper matters.

Once spoken, it was not easy to go back on his word. Lu Yang had no choice but to claim that as a Semi-Immortal, he had to take up the responsibility of guarding the Cultivation World and went to the entrance of the Cultivation World to seek some peace.

At the entrance to the Cultivation World, two layers of defense were established. The first line of defense was made up of Body Integration Realm Cultivators, and the second line was maintained by Pass Tribulation Cultivators, with regular rotations in place to prevent surprise attacks from the Candle Sky Civilization.

Pass Tribulation Cultivators were mostly of the older generation, and Lu Yang was not familiar with them, so he blended in with the team of Integration Period Cultivators—fortunately, he knew some people there.

...

Not far from the Cultivation World, space distorted and a fleet of flesh-like ships emerged through Wormholes.

Eager to reach the Cultivation World as soon as possible, Shi Wumian ordered the fleet to accelerate at all costs. In just under a year, they arrived at their destination.

The moment the spatial jump was complete, Spirit Stone detection radars blared incessantly, and the dial was filled with countless red dots.

Shi Wumian excitedly rubbed his hands together. To him, the sound was incredibly delightful—it meant that the Cultivator named Lu Yang hadn’t deceived the Interstellar Alliance, and the Cultivation World had an inexhaustible supply of Spirit Stones!

Even at Lord Heavenly Emperor’s place of origin, the radar hadn’t reacted so violently!

There might be too many Spirit Stones for all one thousand five hundred warships to carry!

He already envisioned returning fully loaded and the rewards Lord Heavenly Emperor would bestow upon him.

Shi Wumian forced himself to calm down, enlarged the radar dial and projected it onto a screen, so that all the commanders could see.

"You see, the Cultivation World possesses an immense amount of Spirit Stones, but the most numerous and highest quality ones are in these five locations."

Shi Wumian pointed with his baton to five unknown regions, where the red dots were densest and even turned purple.

"In a while, each of you will lead two hundred warships through Directional Wormholes to these five places to plunder the Spirit Stones—take as much as you can!"

"I will report each of your performances to His Majesty the Heavenly Emperor afterward."

In such an uncivilized place, there was no need for rules. Just plunder and that’s it.

"Yes!" freeweɓnovēl.coɱ

The commanders were bright-eyed and excited, realizing that this was an excellent opportunity to establish their careers and compete for the title of Commander in the future.

This is Shi Wumian’s philosophy of using people; only when you give your subordinates benefits, will they be willing to risk their lives for you.

Assigning these five Commanders can maximize the merit they accrue.

Directional wormholes, a type of wormhole technology that even the Interstellar Alliance has yet to master. As long as the probe can determine the location, there’s no need to set up a signal receiver at the other end; directly constructing a wormhole can ensure arrival at the destination.

Five directional wormholes appeared in front of the fleet, and the Commanders led their warships into the wormholes. The wormholes closed, and the fleet vanished.

Shi Wumian’s fleet consisted of 1,500 warships, of which he dispatched 1,000, leaving him with 500.

It would be unbefitting for the Commander to personally rob others, what he needed to do was to wait for the results here.

"Fleet Two, respond."

The communicator made crackling sounds, but there was no response.

There were precedents of this before, with communications resuming normally at closer distances.

Shi Wumian did not like things being out of control. He ordered the remaining 500 warships to move closer to the Cultivation World.

Fleet One passed through the wormhole with radars nearly bursting at the seams, and the Commander was quite excited; this might be the place with the largest quantity of Spirit Stones out of the five locations.

"Report to the Commander, the area below seems to be an undeveloped remote mountain region, with sparse buildings in the mountains."

The Commander, hearing the report, looked downward. It was true; at a glance, the area was full of mountains with few signs of development. It seemed the people living here were quite primitive.

"Land."

A technician saluted and reported, "Report to the Commander, an abnormal energy field detected, initially suspected to be a natural field formed by the excessive and irregular distribution of local Spirit Stones. The fleet is unable to land."

The energy detection dial showed abnormal data, a situation that had never been encountered before.

The Commander frowned, trouble at a critical moment: "What’s the solution?"

Boom—

An immaculate Energy Beam, long charged, descended from the sky and hit the Sect Protection Array of the Seek Dao Sect, causing slight ripples.

Chasing Moon True Person and Qinghe, who were drinking tea on the snowy mountain, along with River Spirit bathing in the river, all looked up simultaneously at the sky at the oddly shaped fleet, resembling caterpillars, feeling puzzled.

Hadn’t two defensive lines been set up at the entrance? How did this fleet get in?

And were they... attacking the Seek Dao Sect?

Inside Captive Peak, the prisoners hearing the commotion all witnessed this scene, dumbstruck.

Through the newspaper, they were informed about the affairs of the Candle Sky Civilization, but they never imagined that the Candle Sky Civilization would dare to attack the Seek Dao Sect.

Guan Shanhai couldn’t help it and burst into laughter.

Chapter 1315: Chapter 1314: Is This the Level of the Cosmic Dominator?

Not only were the prisoners of Captive Peak bewildered, but even the members of Seek Dao Sect did not expect the Candle Sky Civilization Fleet to come knocking on their doorstep.

Therefore, their first reaction was not intense emotions like anger, but confusion.

"Isn’t that the Candle Sky Civilization Fleet mentioned in the newspapers? How did they end up here?"

"Have I gone mad from practicing too hard? Why do I feel like they’re not that strong?" Disciples of the Seek Dao Sect discussed among themselves. This was not at all what they had heard.

"It must be a feint."

"Report to the Commander, the maximum power energy beam failed to neutralize the force field."

For some reason, the Commander was a bit restless and inexplicably irritable. The subordinate’s question sounded utterly foolish to him, and he ordered in a cold voice.

"I’m not blind. If one shot isn’t enough, then fire ten. If ten aren’t enough, fire a hundred. If that’s still not enough, mobilize the entire fleet’s beams. I refuse to believe that two hundred beams can’t break through this place!"

No one could stop him from seizing the Spirit Stones and claiming the credit!

"Yes, sir!" The subordinate saluted and then hurriedly contacted each captain to prepare their energy cannons.

Boom—

Ten maximum power energy beams were fired simultaneously, striking the Sect Protection Array of Seek Dao Sect, causing ten ripples, and that was all.

"They dare to attack us with this kind of level?" Elders of Seek Dao Sect were surprised, and even the Grand Elder rose from his coffin, ready to take action.

Are they underestimating the Seek Dao Sect that much?

"Don’t act, let me do it!"

"Why? Just because you’re the big brother, you won’t let your brothers have a chance?"

"The opponent might be hiding their abilities. It’s life-threatening for you to go. I am the Sect Leader, and I swear to defend the Sect with my life!"

Elders and Daoist Buyu vied with each other, competing for this opportunity.

Just as the Commander thought this attack also had no effect, he saw the river in the distant mountainous area reversing its flow upwards, forming a curtain of rain and enveloping the fleet.

"What’s happening?"

The fleet was in chaos. How could this river act like it’s alive, flying into the sky? What principle was this? They had never encountered such a situation in their expeditions against other civilizations.

"Look outside, there’s someone!"

"He seems to have weapons, two axes?"

River Spirit held a golden axe and a silver axe, his veins popping and his presence fierce as he flew up into the sky, surrounding the entire fleet.

The Seek Dao Sect was not unaccustomed to being attacked. Previously, the Master of All Laws from Great Yu had launched a sneak attack on the Seek Dao Sect, but such a weak attack was a first for him.

The Sect Protection Array was a part of River Spirit’s body. The fleet’s attacks were like urinating on him—it was a downright insult to him as the Protector of Seek Dao Sect!

"A flying native? Seems like he is one of the stronger ones among the natives, like that Lu Yang."

"Haha, coming here with two axes, do they really think such primitive weapons can deal with us?"

The Candle Sky Soldiers laughed heartily, reminded of the time when they were conquering a primitive planet and the natives threw spears at their warships wearing beast skins.

"Fire the cannons and give him a taste of civilization’s generational gap before he dies." freeweɓnøvel.com

The fleet turned their cannons, energy beams gathered, and a shot was fired at River Spirit.

Swish—

A flash of golden light, the energy beam was split in two, and the warships along this straight line were cut neatly in half, the cross-sections smooth and flat, and the wreckage of the warships and Candle Sky Soldiers fell downwards like dumplings.

Dead silence over the fleet communication.

Their warships could only be damaged with a gap by Annihilation Star Weapons and were capable of self-repair, yet they were powerless against a mere single swing of an axe.

The Commander belatedly realized the situation and ordered loudly:

"Retreat! Retreat quickly!"

But when they tried to maneuver their warships to escape, they found the river reversing its current had encircled them, trapping them in a swamp that made it harder to move the more they struggled.

They were horrified. What kind of tactic was this?

Dean Gao watched this scene, mouth agape for a long time.

He had seen the Candle Sky Civilization Fleet before, and the twelve armies of the Interstellar Alliance were powerless against them.

But in the Cultivation World, the situation was completely reversed. River Spirit alone was crushing these two hundred warships!

The Ether Submachine showed a face full of envy. As a Primordial Spirit itself, could it also become this powerful?

Several high-yield shock bombs were dropped into the sea, sinking continuously, with the surroundings changing constantly. The light went from bright to dark, then from dark to bright again, eventually hitting the roof of the Dragon Palace.

Today was the celebration of the Old Dragon Emperor’s longevity, not a grand birthday, just a simple celebration, where dragon sons and grandsons came to offer their gifts.

With a room full of descendants who were all filial, the Old Dragon Emperor laughed heartily when he saw them.

"Come, let’s toast to the Father Emperor’s longevity!"

The dragon sons and grandsons raised their glasses, with harmonious joy all around.

Bang.

Accompanied by a muffled sound, the ground shook slightly, spilling a few drops of wine from the cups.

The Old Dragon Emperor frowned, somewhat displeased. An accident during the birthday celebration was not a good omen.

He had a premonition and looked up, sensing the presence of the Candle Sky Civilization Fleet.

Transforming into dragons, they soared into the sky.

Seeing this, the dragon sons and grandsons followed behind the Old Dragon Emperor.

The sea region trembled, and sea creatures like shrimp soldiers and crab generals kept away from the area, sensing the presence of the dragons.

The group of dragons ascended, and all spirits made way.

"Report, a severe fluctuation has been detected in the waters below. It appears to be a seabed earthquake caused by the shock bombs."

A mere seabed earthquake couldn’t impact their pride and joy - their warships.

However, as soon as the two warships submerged, a huge whirlpool emerged on the sea surface, accompanied by raging winds and a sudden change in weather.

A ferocious ancient dragon, thousands of feet long, clutched the two warships and leaped out of the water, causing thousand-feet-high waves.

Immediately after that, thousands of dragons took to the sea, surrounding the fleet completely, with dragon roars reverberating through the clouds.

The Candle Sky Civilization’s technological development was biased towards bioengineering. The physical forms of their fleet were actually very sturdy meat masses.

The Old Dragon Emperor clutched the two warships as if they were two pieces of meat.

Dragon might suppressed most creatures, including the Candle Sky Soldiers. They felt the terrifying presence of the dragons, and every cell in their body trembled.

The Old Dragon Emperor held the largest warship, which was the command ship of Fleet Two.

There was a hint of puzzlement in the eyes of the Old Dragon Emperor. Is this the warship of the Cosmic Dominator? It doesn’t feel very strong.

The commander stood still, holding his breath, trying not to look at the giant dragon eyes outside the window, and pretending that there was no one on the command ship, hoping to avoid disaster.

Dragon might caused him to break out in cold sweat, and every part of his body was frantically warning him to flee the scene.

But his instincts told him that against a True Dragon, running away would be a sure path to death!

Suddenly, the walkie-talkie crackled: "Calling Fleet Two, requesting support, the might of the Cultivation World natives far exceeds our expectations!"

At that moment, the commander had the urge to kill.

The Old Dragon Emperor roared, the command ship trembled, and the commander could smell the storm of blood emanating from the Old Dragon Emperor’s mouth.

He was so scared that his eyes rolled back, and he passed out.

Chapter 1316: Chapter 1315: Say, where are your main forces!

Shadows appeared in the sky above the Great Xia Imperial City; they were formed by the third fleet.

The citizens in the city looked up in panic, astounded that the enemy had reached their doorstep!

If one were to name the three wealthiest places in the Imperial City, it would naturally be the Imperial Palace, the Land Money Trade Association, and the old residence of the Meng Family; the third fleet aimed for these places.

However, before the third fleet could take any action, the Imperial Guards, Chamber of Commerce Tributors, and Meng Family Elders, these three forces, made their move all at once.

The commander of the third fleet was jolted, "How can so many people fly?"

"Attack! Do not let them get close, everyone attack!"

Two hundred shots of maximum power energy beams were fired, hitting the cultivators of the three parties and instantaneously, dense smoke covered the area, with rolling dust and smoke.

Seeing these natives foolishly not avoiding the attack, the commander turned from shock to glee.

"Stupid natives, facing an unknown attack without even dodging!"

It seemed that the other party only had smoke bombs?

Why did the other side become immobile just at the probing stage?

The Chamber of Commerce Tributors felt somewhat embarrassed; they day-to-day dined, drank, and cultivated all provided by the Commerce, all for acting at crucial moments to protect the Commerce.

They thought this surprise attack by the Candle Sky Civilization would be their chance to fully commit.

Someone’s quantum communication device vibrated, a friend from the Western Paradise Temple was calling.

Facing the fleet’s surprise attack, the Demon Emperor Zhu Tian decisively transformed into his original Di Jiang form, headless and tailless, his body entirely blood-red and round, with six wings on his back.

If Zhu Tian’s true form were only the size of a palm, anyone would praise its cuteness.

But the problem was that his true form was larger than mountains, his six wings unfolded could block out the sun, and the patterns on their surface were as wide as battleships.

Their attacks couldn’t even singe Zhu Tian’s hair.

One after another, Demon Kings and Demon Emperors took to the skies, transformed into their original forms, and demon energy steamed up above Demon City, bearing the scent of despair.

The citizens of Demon City cheered, praising Demon Emperor Zhu Tian for his wise and valiant leadership, which pleased him greatly.

Naturally, Yun Zhi’s return was accompanied by Yun Mengmeng.

Wu Yao: "..."

Still at a loss for what to say, Wu Yao thought, what kind of comment is that? In terms of fame or status, Lu Yang couldn’t compare to him, and yet it’s spoken as if it’s his honor to be able to exchange blows with Lu Yang.

Doesn’t this young girl know how to speak?

"Second-in-command, are you alright?" Yun Mengmeng patted and searched Lu Yang to check his injuries.

Lu Yang’s face flushed red, hastily retreating from Yun Mengmeng: "I’m fine, I’m fine, what could possibly be wrong with me?"

A bolt from the blue descended, it was the Thunder Tribulation clone of Yingtian Immortal.

He sensed the birth of an Immortal Ascension Tribulation near the Cultivation World, so he sent a clone to investigate, wanting to know who had ascended as an Immortal.

"Who is this person?" Yingtian Immortal asked Lu Yang.

"Emperor Wu Yao of Yu, or you could say Heavenly Emperor Wu Yao."

Yingtian Immortal understood at once; it was him. Did he know the gates to the Cultivation World were open, returning home to visit?

Noticing the Candle Sky Soldier and Integration Period Cultivators, he realized it wasn’t quite so: "It looks like a lot has happened during the time I was absent."

After speaking, he dissipated the clone, sending the information here back to his main body. So much had happened in the Cultivation World, it was time to return and take a look.

Finally, Yun Zhi spoke, but her words sent a chill down his spine: "Senior Wu Yao, you’ve condoned your subordinates in their theft of Spirit Stones from the Cultivation World. Do you have anything to say about it?"

Wu Yao quickly offered a placating smile: "A misunderstanding, it’s all a misunderstanding, Fellow Daoist Yun Zhi. It was all done by my subordinates without my knowledge. The Cultivation World is my home too; had I known they were pillaging Spirit Stones from there, I certainly would not have allowed them to commit such outrageous acts!"

"You see, as soon as I learned they were going to the Cultivation World to steal Spirit Stones, I set out immediately to intercept them. It’s just that they were too far away, and I was one step too late, they still engaged in conflict with the Cultivation World."

Yun Zhi’s eyes slightly lifted, maintaining that unchanging, deep, well-like expression, leaving Wu Yao unable to decipher her thoughts.

"A misunderstanding? So you’re saying, Senior Wu Yao, that your attempt to reclaim your captive and the resulting conflict with my Junior Brother, as well as injuring my Junior Brother, was also a misunderstanding?"

Hearing this, Lu Yang happened to cough a few times, his voice hoarse and heavy, hinting at serious injury, and also coughing up some blood, substantiating the Eldest Senior Sister’s words.

Wu Yao’s eyelids twitched upon hearing the words, and his voice grew icy, abandoning his previously ingratiating demeanor: "So, you mean to say, Daoist Yun Zhi insists on not letting this matter go?"

"The incident has happened; naturally, there must be an explanation. Wu Yao, Senior, you are welcome to discuss this at Captive Peak within the Seek Dao Sect."

"Don’t go too far!" Wu Yao bellowed in anger, fully aware of what kind of place Captive Peak was.

Who is he? Having cultivated to become an Immortal in two lifetimes, he’s the only one since ancient times to have achieved this. As an Immortal who transcends the mortal world, when has one ever heard of an Immortal being reduced to a mere prisoner? It would be an immense humiliation!

He had previously thought to avoid conflict for the sake of profit, not wishing to provoke a formidable enemy like Yun Zhi over trifles.

But if Yun Zhi thinks she can arbitrarily decide his fate, then she is gravely mistaken.

At this moment, he is at the peak of his life. He is far stronger than when he was Emperor Wu Yao, not only in terms of Mind State but also the disparity within the Dao Fruits. He is a Heavenly Emperor in the truest sense, and if a fight were to erupt, he would fear no one!

Simultaneously, he covertly stimulated the Creation Dao Fruit, predicting the outcome of this potential battle.

"After this battle, I will be able to comprehend true principles, reunite with dear friends and mentors after more than a hundred thousand years, clash with other Immortals, and exchange insights on the Immortal Dao, filling in what I lack?"

"What great fortune, what a grand opportunity this is!"

When the Dao Fruit was merely an outline, his clash with Lu Yang let him vaguely sense that Lu Yang would bring him great fortune. Albeit this premonition was faint, once the Dao Fruit formed, his sensitivity to fortune and opportunity became much clearer, a sort of prediction of the future!

Assured by the results given by the Dao Fruit, Wu Yao was full of confidence. Such gains must not be missed from this opportunity.

The fight must happen now if at all; upon learning of this place, the Thunder Tribulation clone of the Yingtian Immortal will surely return to the Cultivation World. And if Yun Zhi were to join forces with the Four Ancient Immortals, he would certainly be no match.

The bronze spear reappeared, its might extraordinary. The Creation Dao Fruit easily advanced the spear, transforming it from an Immortal Treasure into a true Immortal Artifact.

As the spear danced, it emitted a light that resembled hanging galaxies, demonstrating the vast difference between Immortal Treasures and true Immortal Artifacts with just this one move.

The Creation Dao Fruit unveiled its divine power, with myriad monsters leaping out of the painting-like Fish Leaping Over the Dragon’s Gate, appearing even more formidable than legends suggested. Despite not stepping into the Immortal Level, they already subtly bore the grace of Immortality.

The bronze spear, too, was replicated by the mere thought into millions of copies, hanging throughout space.

Immortal Talismans, Immortal-level Arrays... they overwhelmed the sky, submerging the area.

The Integration Period Cultivators and the Transcendance Tribulation Stage ones were utterly astonished by this scene. Wasn’t the fighting supposed to have stopped? Why has it suddenly escalated again?

Seeing the extent of preparations, it was clear that serious engagement was imminent, but Wu Yao was already an Immortal; who present here was worth his true effort?

"Daoist Yun Zhi, you will regret your decision today!" Wu Yao’s brow bore the mark of an Immortal pattern, controlling all of Creation. Having become an Immortal, his Spiritual Sense metamorphosed into Immortal Sense, the might of which was boundless.

Purple qi rose tumultuously, chaos pervaded, and with creation through Immortal Dao, he attacked Yun Zhi, showcasing the majesty of an Immortal!

"Cloud Falling Palm."

Yun Zhi responded indifferently to Wu Yao’s roar, her single hand shattering his Immortal Creation.

Wu Yao watched powerlessly as the delicate hand fell, unstoppable, regret and despair surging from the depths of his heart.

Was the gap between him and Yun Zhi still so vast?

Boom—

Immortal Creation shattered, and all returned to calm.

Wu Yao, lifted by Yun Zhi, had a vacant look, his clarity gone. At this moment, he finally understood a lesson—not to take one’s dignity too seriously, for there will be times when one is shamed.
